  },

  // ąöąö CRM Query Planner (read-only, not review-gated) ąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąö
  // Agent-facing tool per spec čģ18.2 - dispatches through the planner
  // pipeline (Stage 1 registry / Stage 2 cache / Stage 3 LLM fallback /
  // canonical + live + hybrid executors) and returns the BriefResultContract
  // artefact set. The route at /api/crm-query-planner/query is the user
  // surface; this handler is the agent surface.
  'crm.query': async (input, context) => {
    // Resolve target subaccount - prefer the explicit tool-input value,
    // falling back to the agent's bound subaccount context.
    const suppliedSubaccountId = typeof input.subaccountId === 'string' && input.subaccountId.length > 0
      ? input.subaccountId
      : null;
    const targetSubaccountId = suppliedSubaccountId ?? context.subaccountId;

    if (!targetSubaccountId) {
      return {
        success: false,
        error:   'missing_permission',
        message: 'crm.query requires a subaccount - supply input.subaccountId or bind the agent to a subaccount.',
      };
    }

    // Horizontal-access guard (mirrors intelligenceSkillExecutor.executeQuerySubaccountCohort):
    // a regular subaccount agent may only read its own subaccount. Only
    // org-subaccount agents (allowedSubaccountIds === null) may cross
    // boundaries, and even then only to subaccounts in their allowlist if
    // the array form is present. Skip when the caller made no explicit
    // cross-subaccount request (input.subaccountId matches context or was omitted).
    if (suppliedSubaccountId && suppliedSubaccountId !== context.subaccountId) {
      const allowed = context.allowedSubaccountIds;
      const isOrgScope = allowed === null || allowed === undefined;
      const inAllowlist = Array.isArray(allowed) && allowed.includes(suppliedSubaccountId);
      if (!isOrgScope && !inAllowlist) {
        return {
          success: false,
          error:   'missing_permission',
          message: 'Agent is not authorised to read the specified subaccount.',
        };
      }
    }

    const { runQuery } = await import('./crmQueryPlanner/index.js');
    const result = await runQuery(
      {
        rawIntent:    String(input.rawIntent ?? ''),
        subaccountId: targetSubaccountId,
        briefId:      typeof input.briefId === 'string' ? input.briefId : undefined,
      },
      {
        orgId:                  context.organisationId,
        organisationId:         context.organisationId,
        subaccountId:           targetSubaccountId,
        runId:                  context.runId,
        briefId:                typeof input.briefId === 'string' ? input.briefId : undefined,
        principalType:          'agent',
        principalId:            context.agentId,
        teamIds:                [],
        // Agent-invoked - the agent's own capabilityMap gated the skill
        // dispatch upstream (skillExecutor.execute). The planner's
        // validator treats unknown `canonical.*` slugs as skipped per
        // čģ12.1, so the route's subaccount-capability union is not
        // required here - `crm.query` is the only hard-gated slug.
        callerCapabilities:     new Set<string>(['crm.query']),
        defaultSenderIdentifier: undefined,
      },
    );
    return { success: true, ...result };
  },

  notify_operator: async (input, context) => {
    return proposeReviewGatedAction('notify_operator', input, context);
  },

  // ąöąö Phase 3 S22: Deliver Workflow output via deliveryService ąöąöąöąöąö
  config_deliver_workflow_output: async (input, context) => {
    const { deliveryService } = await import('./deliveryService.js');
    const {
      subaccountId,
      organisationId,
      artefactTitle,
      artefactContent,
      deliveryChannels,
    } = input as Record<string, unknown>;

    if (!subaccountId || !organisationId || !artefactTitle || !artefactContent) {
      return { success: false, error: 'subaccountId, organisationId, artefactTitle, artefactContent required' };
    }

    const config =
      (deliveryChannels as { email?: boolean; portal?: boolean; slack?: boolean } | undefined) ??
      { email: true, portal: true, slack: false };

    const result = await deliveryService.deliver(
      {
        title: String(artefactTitle),
        content: String(artefactContent),
        createdByAgentId: context.agentId,
      },
      {
        email: Boolean(config.email ?? true),
        portal: Boolean(config.portal ?? true),
        slack: Boolean(config.slack ?? false),
      },
      String(subaccountId),
      String(organisationId),
    );

    return {
      success: true,
      taskId: result.taskId,
      channels: result.channels,
    };
  },

  // ąöąö Sprint 5 P4.2: Memory block write path ąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąö
  update_memory_block: async (input, context) => {
    const { updateBlock } = await import('./memoryBlockService.js');
    const blockName = (input as Record<string, unknown>).block_name as string;
    const newContent = (input as Record<string, unknown>).new_content as string;
    if (!blockName || !newContent) {
      return { success: false, error: 'block_name and new_content are required' };
    }
    return updateBlock(blockName, newContent, context.agentId, context.organisationId);
  },

export const skillExecutor = {
  async execute(params: SkillExecutionParams): Promise<unknown> {
    const { skillName, input, context, toolCallId } = params;
    // Stash the current tool call id on the context so the per-case
    // action wrappers below can build the same deterministic idempotency
    // key that proposeActionMiddleware wrote for this call (Sprint 2 P1.1
    // Layer 3). Mutation is safe - the context is scoped to one run and
    // one tool call at a time.
    if (toolCallId !== undefined) {
      context.toolCallId = toolCallId;
    }

    // MCP tool dispatch - tool slugs start with "mcp."
    if (skillName.startsWith('mcp.') && context._mcpClients) {
      const { mcpClientManager } = await import('./mcpClientManager.js');
      return mcpClientManager.callTool(
        context._mcpClients,
        context._mcpLazyRegistry ?? new Map(),
        skillName,
        input,
        {
          runId: context.runId,
          organisationId: context.organisationId,
          agentId: context.agentId,
          subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
          isTestRun: context.isTestRun ?? false,
          taskId: context.taskId,
          mcpCallCount: context.mcpCallCount,
        },
      );
    }

    const handler = SKILL_HANDLERS[skillName];
    if (!handler) {
      return { success: false, error: `Unknown skill: ${skillName}` };
    }
    return handler(input, context);
  },
};

  // ąöąö Sub-Account Optimiser: generic agent-output primitive (Chunk 1) ąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąö
  // output.recommend - any agent with this skill can surface operator-facing
  // recommendations via the generic agent_recommendations primitive.
  // Spec: docs/sub-account-optimiser-spec.md čģ6.2
  'output.recommend': async (input, context) => {
    // Requires an agent execution context - non-agent callers are rejected.
    if (!context.agentId) {
      return {
        success: false,
        error: 'output.recommend requires an agent execution context (agentId missing)',
      };
    }

    const {
      scope_type,
      scope_id,
      category,
      severity,
      title,
      body,
      evidence,
      action_hint,
      dedupe_key,
    } = input as Record<string, unknown>;

    // Validate required fields
    if (!scope_type || (scope_type !== 'org' && scope_type !== 'subaccount')) {
      return { success: false, error: 'scope_type must be "org" or "subaccount"' };
    }
    if (!scope_id || typeof scope_id !== 'string') {
      return { success: false, error: 'scope_id must be a valid UUID string' };
    }
    // Basic UUID validation
    const uuidRegex = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i;
    if (!uuidRegex.test(scope_id)) {
      return { success: false, error: 'scope_id must be a valid UUID' };
    }
    if (!severity || !['info', 'warn', 'critical'].includes(severity as string)) {
      return { success: false, error: 'severity must be "info", "warn", or "critical"' };
    }
    if (!category || typeof category !== 'string') {
      return { success: false, error: 'category is required' };
    }
    // Validate three-segment format
    const categoryParts = (category as string).split('.');
    if (categoryParts.length < 3) {
      return {
        success: false,
        error: 'category must follow <agent_namespace>.<area>.<finding> format (three segments)',
      };
    }
    if (!title || typeof title !== 'string') {
      return { success: false, error: 'title is required' };
    }
    if (!body || typeof body !== 'string') {
      return { success: false, error: 'body is required' };
    }
    if (!evidence || typeof evidence !== 'object' || Array.isArray(evidence)) {
      return { success: false, error: 'evidence must be a plain object' };
    }
    if (!dedupe_key || typeof dedupe_key !== 'string') {
      return { success: false, error: 'dedupe_key is required' };
    }
    // Validate action_hint: null/omitted accepted; non-null must match scheme://path format
    if (action_hint !== undefined && action_hint !== null) {
      if (typeof action_hint !== 'string' || action_hint === '') {
        return { success: false, error: 'action_hint must be null/omitted or a non-empty URI string' };
      }
      const actionHintRegex = /^[a-z][a-z0-9-]*:\/\/[^\s]+$/;
      if (!actionHintRegex.test(action_hint as string)) {
        return {
          success: false,
          error: 'action_hint must match pattern ^[a-z][a-z0-9-]*://[^\\s]+$ (e.g. configuration-assistant://agent/id?focus=budget)',
        };
      }
    }

    const { upsertRecommendation } = await import('./agentRecommendationsService.js');
    const result = await upsertRecommendation(
      {
        organisationId: context.organisationId,
        agentId: context.agentId,
      },
      {
        scope_type: scope_type as 'org' | 'subaccount',
        scope_id: scope_id as string,
        category: category as string,
        severity: severity as 'info' | 'warn' | 'critical',
        title: title as string,
        body: body as string,
        evidence: evidence as Record<string, unknown>,
        action_hint: (action_hint as string | null | undefined) ?? null,
        dedupe_key: dedupe_key as string,
      },
    );
    return { success: true, ...result };
  },

  // ąöąö Thread context (Chunk A - per-conversation living doc) ąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąö
  update_thread_context: async (input, context) => {
    if (!context.conversationId) {
      return { success: false, error: 'update_thread_context requires a conversation context - this run has no associated conversation.' };
    }
    return executeWithActionAudit('update_thread_context', input, context, () =>
      updateThreadContextHandler(input, {
        conversationId: context.conversationId!,
        runId: context.runId,
        organisationId: context.organisationId,
        subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
      }),
    );
  },

  // ąöąö Sub-Account Optimiser: scan skills (Chunk 5) ąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąöąö
  // Each scan skill is a thin wrapper: query module  evaluator  EvaluatorOutput[].
  // All scan skills are read-only (no action record, no side effects).
  // Spec: docs/sub-account-optimiser-spec.md čģ5

  'optimiser.scan_agent_budget': async (input, context) => {
    const subaccountId = requireSubaccountContext(context, 'optimiser.scan_agent_budget');
    try {
      const { module: agentBudgetModule } = await import('./optimiser/queries/agentBudget.js');
      const { evaluate } = await import('./optimiser/recommendations/agentBudget.js');
      const tx = getOrgScopedDb('optimiser.scan_agent_budget');
      const rows = await agentBudgetModule.run(tx, subaccountId);
      logger.info('optimiser.scan.completed', { scanCategory: agentBudgetModule.category, resultCount: rows.length, subaccountId });
      const outputs = evaluate(rows, { subaccountId, organisationId: context.organisationId, medianVersion: 0, priorRecsByDedupe: new Map() });
      return { success: true, outputs };
    } catch (err) {
      logger.error('optimiser.scan.failed', { scanCategory: 'optimiser.agent.over_budget', error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err), subaccountId });
      throw err;
    }
  },

  'optimiser.scan_workflow_escalations': async (input, context) => {
    const subaccountId = requireSubaccountContext(context, 'optimiser.scan_workflow_escalations');
    try {
      const { module: escalationRateModule } = await import('./optimiser/queries/escalationRate.js');
      const { evaluate } = await import('./optimiser/recommendations/playbookEscalation.js');

  'optimiser.scan_skill_latency': async (input, context) => {
    const subaccountId = requireSubaccountContext(context, 'optimiser.scan_skill_latency');
    try {
      const { skillLatencyModule, peerMediansViewIsPopulated, runSkillLatencyQuery } = await import('./optimiser/queries/skillLatency.js');
      const { evaluateSkillSlow } = await import('./optimiser/recommendations/skillSlow.js');
      // peerMediansViewIsPopulated manages its own admin connection internally
      const populated = await peerMediansViewIsPopulated();
      if (!populated) {
        logger.info('optimiser.scan.partial', { scanCategory: skillLatencyModule.category, medianVersion: 0, subaccountId });
        return { success: true, outputs: [] };
      }
      // allowRlsBypass: reading cross-tenant peer medians view (optimiser_skill_peer_medians) - read-only aggregate, no tenant data written
      const { withAdminConnectionGuarded: adminGuarded } = await import('../lib/rlsBoundaryGuard.js');
      let outputs: import('./optimiser/recommendations/types.js').EvaluatorOutput[] = [];
      await adminGuarded(
        { source: 'optimiser.scan_skill_latency', allowRlsBypass: false },
        async (adminTx) => {
          const versionRows = await adminTx.execute<{ max_version: number }>(
            (await import('drizzle-orm')).sql`SELECT MAX(median_version) AS max_version FROM optimiser_skill_peer_medians`,
          );
          const medianVersion = versionRows[0]?.max_version ?? 0;
          const rows = await runSkillLatencyQuery(adminTx, subaccountId, medianVersion);
          logger.info('optimiser.scan.completed', { scanCategory: skillLatencyModule.category, resultCount: rows.length, subaccountId });
          outputs = evaluateSkillSlow(rows, { subaccountId, organisationId: context.organisationId, medianVersion, priorRecsByDedupe: new Map() });
        },
      );
      return { success: true, outputs };
    } catch (err) {
      logger.error('optimiser.scan.failed', { scanCategory: 'optimiser.skill.slow', error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err), subaccountId });
      throw err;
    }
  },

// Converts a SkillExecutionContext to a ServicePrincipal for support service calls.
function buildSupportPrincipal(context: SkillExecutionContext): import('./principal/types.js').PrincipalContext {
  return {
    type: 'service',
    id: context.agentId,
    organisationId: context.organisationId,
    subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
    serviceId: 'support-skill',
    teamIds: [],
  };
}

## 6. Current State (Brief)

`server/services/skillExecutor.ts` is 6,133 LOC. It conflates seven concerns:

1. **Public-surface declarations**: the `SkillExecutionContext` interface (exported, lines 137-229), the private `SkillExecutionParams` interface (declared but not exported, lines 231-243 ŲÆ?" argument shape of `skillExecutor.execute`), and the `SkillHandler` type alias (exported, lines 426-429).
2. **Module-load side effects** (lines 60-131): `registerAdapter('worker', ...)` dispatch switch ŲÆ?" the review-gated worker handler. The switch covers ~20 action-type cases, mostly delegating to in-file `*Approved` executors, but also routes `create_page`/`update_page`/`publish_page` to in-file (non-`*Approved`) page executors, and dispatches `config_update_organisation_config` + `notify_operator` via inline `await import(...)` of sibling services.
3. **Pipeline orchestration** (lines 257-414): `applyOnFailure`, `runWithProcessors`, `processorRegistry`, `registerProcessor`, `setHandoffJobSender`, on-failure dispatch.
4. **Handler registry** (lines 439-2493): the `SKILL_HANDLERS` constant ŲÆ?" built in THREE pieces, not one: the main literal at line 439 (~1,700 lines, most slugs), an `Object.assign(SKILL_HANDLERS, {...})` block at line 2210 (10 `support.*` slugs), and another `Object.assign(SKILL_HANDLERS, {...})` block at line 2374 (11 `calendar.*` + `slack.*` slugs). Total ~200 slugs. The ┬Č├Ą7 Chunk 14 (registry assembly) consolidates these three pieces into a single assembled map via the spread pattern.
5. **Gate / audit wrappers** (lines 2547-2823): `executeWithActionAudit`, `proposeReviewGatedAction`, `awaitReviewDecision`, `buildDenialMessage`.
6. **Per-handler implementations** (lines 2825-6133): ~50 individual async functions ŲÆ?" `executeWebSearch`, `executeReadWorkspace`, `executeWriteWorkspace`, `executeCreateTask`, `executeMoveTask`, `executeReassignTask`, `executeSpawnSubAgents`, `executeFetchUrl`, `executeScrapeUrl`, `executeScrapeStructured`, `executeMonitorWebpage`, `executeReadCodebase`, `executeSearchCodebase`, `executeRunTests`, `executeAnalyzeEndpoint`, `executeReportBug`, `executeCaptureScreenshot`, `executeRunPlaywrightTest`, `executeCreatePage` / `executeUpdatePage` / `executePublishPage`, the methodology skills, the Workflow Studio executors, `executeImportN8nWorkflow`, the worker-approved-execute stubs for 10+ action types.
7. **One-off helpers** (locations in source): `requireSubaccountContext` (line 250), `buildSupportPrincipal` (line 2197 ŲÆ?" used by all support.* handlers), `resolveAgentOwner` (line 2356 ŲÆ?" used by all calendar.* and slack.* handlers), `serializeTask` (line 2965), `redactSensitiveFields` (line 3312 ŲÆ?" used by `executeDocProposalApproved`/`executeWriteDocsApproved`), `buildIdeaDescription`/`buildBugDescription`/`buildChoreDescription`/`inferTypeFromDescription`/`suggestDisposition` (lines 3617-3736 ŲÆ?" used by `executeTriageIntake`), `deriveSelectorGroup` (line 4790 ŲÆ?" used by `executeScrapeUrl`), `proposeDevopsAction` (line 5210 ŲÆ?" used by devContext handlers).

The seven concerns map cleanly to the ┬Č├Ą5.2 module tree. No two concerns are entangled at runtime ŲÆ?" the only shared mutable state is the processor registry and pg-boss sender, both of which move to `pipeline.ts`.

## 7. Chunked Migration Plan

Each chunk is a complete, independently-mergeable PR (squashable into the integration branch). Builders execute one chunk at a time; G1 runs after each. The order is dependency-driven ŲÆ?" early chunks land foundation pieces that later chunks consume.

**Sequencing rule for the worker-adapter `registerAdapter('worker', ...)` call.** The dispatch switch (lines 69-131 of the current file) is a module-load side effect that references several handler functions by name. While those handler functions are still private to the barrel (chunks 1-12 in this plan), the `registerAdapter(...)` call STAYS at the top of the barrel ŲÆ?" extracting it earlier would require either (a) re-exporting private handlers from the barrel transitionally, or (b) having `adapter-registration.ts` import the barrel itself, both of which violate ┬Č├Ą5.3. The adapter-registration module is therefore extracted in Chunk 13, after `handlers/pages.ts` (Chunk 9) and `handlers/delegation.ts` (Chunk 12) both exist and export the named handlers it needs.

### Chunk 1 ŲÆ?" Scaffold + types (foundation)

- Create the `server/services/skillExecutor/` directory.
- Create `skillExecutor/context.ts` and move `SkillExecutionContext`, `SkillHandler`, `requireSubaccountContext` from the barrel.
- `SkillExecutionParams` does NOT move here ŲÆ?" it stays in the barrel for now and migrates to `registry.ts` in Chunk 14 alongside the `skillExecutor` object that consumes it (private symbol, no public-surface impact).
- Update `skillExecutor.ts` to re-export the moved types from `context.ts`. Public surface preserved.
- Update one canonical importer (`agentExecutionLoop.ts`) to import the type from the new path as a smoke test. All other importers keep using the barrel re-export.
- G1 success criteria: lint, typecheck, build:server pass. No behaviour change.

### Chunk 2 ŲÆ?" Pipeline module

- Create `skillExecutor/pipeline.ts` containing: `processorRegistry`, `runWithProcessors`, `registerProcessor`, `applyOnFailure`, `applyOnFailureForStructuredFailure`, `setHandoffJobSender`, `pgBossSend` private state, `enqueueHandoff`, `AGENT_HANDOFF_QUEUE` constant.
- Pipeline imports per ┬Č├Ą5.3 ŲÆ?" including the DB/schema imports `enqueueHandoff` needs (`db`, `subaccountAgents`, `agents`, `agentRuns`, `eq`, `and`, `isActive`, `MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH`, `createEvent`).
- Update barrel to re-export `registerProcessor` and `setHandoffJobSender` from `pipeline.ts`.
- G1: lint, typecheck, build:server, targeted run of any `processorRegistry`/`enqueueHandoff` unit test.

### Chunk 3 ŲÆ?" Gating module

- Create `skillExecutor/gating.ts` containing: `executeWithActionAudit`, `proposeReviewGatedAction`, `awaitReviewDecision`, `buildDenialMessage`.
- Gating imports `pipeline.ts` for `runWithProcessors`.
- No public surface change ŲÆ?" these were already internal.
- G1: lint, typecheck, build:server.

### Chunks 4-10 ŲÆ?" Handler families (one chunk per family)

Each chunk moves one `handlers/<family>.ts` worth of code out of the barrel:

| Chunk | Family | Skills / functions moved |
|---|---|---|
| 4 | `handlers/web.ts` | `web_search`/`executeWebSearch` + `logSearchUsage`, `fetch_url`/`executeFetchUrl`, `scrape_url`/`executeScrapeUrl` + `deriveSelectorGroup`, `scrape_structured`/`executeScrapeStructured`, `monitor_webpage`/`executeMonitorWebpage`, `capture_screenshot`/`executeCaptureScreenshot`, `run_playwright_test`/`executeRunPlaywrightTest`, `analyze_endpoint`/`executeAnalyzeEndpoint` |

(`report_bug`/`executeReportBug` lives in `handlers/tasks.ts` per Chunk 6 ŲÆ?" it creates a board task and uses task-service primitives, even though the source happens to place it near the dev-context family at line 5569.) |

The `executeMethodologySkill` helper function itself moves with `methodologyStubs.ts` in Chunk 10a ŲÆ?" NOT with this chunk; `pages.ts` is page-specific only. Per-chunk procedure:
1. Move the named functions and any helpers used only by them into the new file.
2. Update the slot in the in-barrel `SKILL_HANDLERS` literal to import from the new file (still in the barrel at this point).
3. Builder runs G1 (lint + typecheck + build:server). No targeted tests required unless a handler-specific test exists.
4. PR description names every moved function and every consumer updated.

### Chunks 10aŲÆ?"10e ŲÆ?" Stub-family and thin-shell modules

These chunks land the high-volume "everything else" slugs identified in ┬Č├Ą5.2.1. The numbering uses `10a` ŲÆ?├Ø `10e` (decimal sub-chunks) to keep downstream chunk numbers stable; the operator may also collapse adjacent ones into a single PR if the diff is small.

| Chunk | Module | Approx slug count |
|---|---|---|
| 10a | `handlers/methodologyStubs.ts` | ~30 (every `executeMethodologySkill` consumer) |
| 10b | `handlers/autoGatedStubs.ts` + `handlers/reviewGatedProposers.ts` | ~25 combined (every inline `executeWithActionAudit` stub and every inline `proposeReviewGatedAction` gate) |
| 10c | `handlers/systemMonitorShells.ts` + `handlers/optimiserShells.ts` + `handlers/spendShells.ts` + `handlers/configShells.ts` + `handlers/capabilityDiscovery.ts` | ~55 combined (thin shells over already-extracted sibling services) |
| 10d | `handlers/crm.ts` + `handlers/orgInsights.ts` + `handlers/output.ts` + `handlers/threadContext.ts` + `handlers/notifyOperator.ts` + `handlers/memoryBlock.ts` + `handlers/financialReporting.ts` | ~25 combined |
| 10e | `handlers/mediaTranscription.ts` + `handlers/digest.ts` + `handlers/thinDispatchers.ts` (catch-all for any leftover thin dispatchers) | ~10 combined |

Per-sub-chunk procedure is the same as Chunks 4-10 above: move the slugs to the new file, update the in-barrel `SKILL_HANDLERS` literal slot, G1 the chunk. Each sub-chunk PR description enumerates the exact slug set moved.

After Chunk 10e lands, the in-barrel `SKILL_HANDLERS` literal is empty (every slug has moved to a `handlers/*` module). The next chunks (11, 12, 13, 14, 15) operate on the now-emptied registry.

### Chunk 11 ŲÆ?" Remaining handler shells (small)

- `handlers/memory.ts`, `handlers/slack.ts`, `handlers/calendar.ts`, `handlers/support.ts`, `handlers/meta.ts`, `handlers/capabilities.ts`. These are largely thin re-exports / dynamic-import sites today; the chunk consolidates them.
- The `buildSupportPrincipal` helper moves to `handlers/support.ts` next to its consumers. The 10 support.* slugs in the `Object.assign(SKILL_HANDLERS, {...})` block at lines 2210-2349 (`support.list_open_tickets`, `support.read_thread`, `support.propose_reply`, `support.add_internal_note`, `support.approve_draft`, `support.reject_draft`, `support.set_status`, `support.assign`, `support.tag`, `support.find_customer_history`) plus the inline `support.classify_ticket` slug at line 840 (a thin dispatcher to `skillHandlers/supportClassifyTicket.ts`) all land in `handlers/support.ts` (11 slugs total).
- The `resolveAgentOwner` helper (used by all calendar.* and slack.* handlers) lands in a small shared module `skillExecutor/handlers/userOwnedAgentOwner.ts`. Both `handlers/calendar.ts` and `handlers/slack.ts` import it. This is the same one-way edge pattern ┬Č├Ą5.3 allows (e.g. `tasks.ts ŲÆ├ģ' handoff.ts` for `enqueueHandoff`).
- The line-2374 `Object.assign(SKILL_HANDLERS, {...})` block contains the calendar.* and slack.* slugs ŲÆ?" naming for clarity: `calendar.list_events`, `calendar.get_event`, `calendar.find_free_slot`, `calendar.create_event`, `calendar.update_event`, `calendar.respond_to_invite` (6 calendar slugs), `slack.list_channels`, `slack.read_channel`, `slack.search_messages`, `slack.summarise_thread`, `slack.post_message`, `slack.post_dm` (6 slack slugs). Move all 12 into `handlers/calendar.ts` / `handlers/slack.ts` as part of this chunk.
- G1: lint, typecheck, build:server.

### Chunk 12 ŲÆ?" Worker-approved-execute family (delegation handlers)

- Create `skillExecutor/handlers/delegation.ts` containing: `executeWriteSpecApproved`, `executePublishPostApproved`, `executeAdsActionApproved`, `executeCrmUpdateApproved`, `executeFinancialRecordUpdateApproved`, `executeLeadMagnetApproved`, `executeDeliverReportApproved`, `executeConfigureIntegrationApproved`, `executeDocProposalApproved`, `executeWriteDocsApproved`, plus `redactSensitiveFields`.
- The barrel's `registerAdapter('worker', ...)` call now references these from `handlers/delegation.ts` directly (still inline at the top of the barrel; the dispatch switch updates its imports but stays in `skillExecutor.ts` for now). This is the last "in-barrel" mutation before the adapter call is extracted in Chunk 13.
- G1: lint, typecheck, build:server. Functional: confirm worker dispatch still fires through `registerAdapter('worker', ...)`.

### Chunk 13 ŲÆ?" Extract adapter-registration

- Now that `handlers/pages.ts` (Chunk 9) and `handlers/delegation.ts` (Chunk 12) both exist, the `registerAdapter('worker', ...)` call moves out of the barrel into `skillExecutor/adapter-registration.ts`.
- `adapter-registration.ts` imports per ┬Č├Ą5.3: `executionLayerService.registerAdapter`, `adapters/workerAdapter.createWorkerAdapter`, `config/actionRegistry.resolveActionSlug`, `context.ts` (for `SkillExecutionContext`), the three page executors from `handlers/pages.ts`, and the worker-approved executors from `handlers/delegation.ts`. The two dynamic-import dispatch arms (`config_update_organisation_config`, `notify_operator`) stay as inline `await import(...)`.
- The barrel adds `import './skillExecutor/adapter-registration.js';` at the top (side-effect import ŲÆ?" preserves the load-time `registerAdapter` invariant).
- G1: lint, typecheck, build:server. Functional: emit a synthetic worker action in a test environment to confirm the adapter still fires. (CI gates cover the contract assertion.)

### Chunk 14 ŲÆ?" Registry assembly + barrel thinning

- Create `skillExecutor/registry.ts` exporting `SKILL_HANDLERS` assembled from `handlers/*` imports. The three-piece source-file shape (one literal + two `Object.assign(SKILL_HANDLERS, {...})` blocks at lines 2210 and 2374) consolidates into a single assembled `Record<string, SkillHandler>` ŲÆ?" the spread pattern (`{ ...webHandlers, ...workspaceHandlers, ...taskHandlers, ... }`) replaces the in-place `Object.assign`.
- Move the `skillExecutor` object constant (`{ execute }`) AND the private `SkillExecutionParams` interface to `registry.ts` so the closure stays in the same module.
- Update the barrel `skillExecutor.ts` to its final shape per ┬Č├Ą5.7.
- G1: lint, typecheck, build:server. Targeted run of `__tests__/skillHandlerRegistryEquivalence.test.ts` to confirm `SKILL_HANDLERS` slug set is unchanged.
- G2 (integrated): full lint + typecheck + build:server + build:client (no client changes expected; this is the "did we break a transitive import" check).

### Chunk 15 ŲÆ?" Caller sweep + doc sync

- Sweep callers (┬Č├Ą10 / ┬Č├Ą4 list). Where a caller imports a type that has moved, optionally update the caller to point at the new canonical path; otherwise leave the caller on the barrel re-export.
- Update `architecture.md ┬Č├Ą Skill executor & processor hooks` to describe the new module tree (one short paragraph and a pointer to the directory).
- Update `docs/doc-sync.md` if needed (likely not ŲÆ?" the rule already covers this).
- G2 final: lint, typecheck, build:server, build:client.

A slug that calls `await import('./otherService.js')` and forwards lives in `handlers/thinDispatchers.ts` unless its sibling service has a natural family home (then it goes in that family's module instead ąō?" e.g. spend dispatchers go to `spendShells.ts`, config dispatchers to `configShells.ts`, system-monitor dispatchers to `systemMonitorShells.ts`, optimiser dispatchers to `optimiserShells.ts`).

This rule ensures every one of the 214 slugs maps to exactly one `handlers/<family>.ts` module, no slug stays inline in `registry.ts` after Chunk 14. If a future audit finds a slug not covered, it goes into the closest-fit module from the list above OR a new family module is added with a follow-up chunk; the spec's invariant is "no inline handlers in `registry.ts` post-split", not "exactly these modules forever".

### 5.3. Dependency direction (DAG, no cycles)

```
                        ąō"Oąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?

                                 ąō"' re-exports

              ąō"Oąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"ą╝ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?ąō"?

              ąō"'                  ąō"'                  ąō"'

                  (skillExecutorPure,         (handlers/* MAY import other
                   delegationPure,            services and other handlers,
                   future Pure helpers)       but NEVER the barrel)
```

Concrete rules:
- The barrel `skillExecutor.ts` imports from `skillExecutor/registry`, `skillExecutor/context`, `skillExecutor/pipeline`, `skillExecutor/gating`, and `skillExecutor/adapter-registration` (last one for side effect only). NOTHING else.
- `context.ts` is a leaf ąō?" imports types only from `../../shared/types/**` and external libs. NO imports from `db`, `services`, or sibling sub-modules.
- `pipeline.ts` imports `context.ts`, `skillExecutorPure.ts`, `actionRegistry`, `tracing` (for `createEvent`), `tripwire`, `incidentIngestor`, and the imports `enqueueHandoff` needs today ąō?" `db`, drizzle helpers (`eq`, `and`), `lib/queryHelpers` (`isActive`), the schema tables `subaccountAgents` / `agents` / `agentRuns`, and `config/limits` (`MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH`). The `AGENT_HANDOFF_QUEUE` constant lives in `pipeline.ts` alongside `enqueueHandoff`. It does NOT import from `gating.ts` or any `handlers/*` (the gating module is a consumer of pipeline, not a peer).
- `gating.ts` imports `context.ts`, `pipeline.ts`, `actionService`, `reviewService`, `hitlService`, `executionLayerService`, `actionRegistry`, `tracing`. It does NOT import any `handlers/*`.
- Every `handlers/*.ts` imports `context.ts` (for the type), `gating.ts` (for `executeWithActionAudit` / `proposeReviewGatedAction`), and whatever services it dispatches to. It does NOT import any other `handlers/*` module, with two narrow exceptions: (a) `handlers/calendar.ts` and `handlers/slack.ts` may import `handlers/userOwnedAgentOwner.ts` for the shared `resolveAgentOwner` helper, and (b) `handlers/tasks.ts` and `handlers/handoff.ts` both import `enqueueHandoff` from `pipeline.ts` (per ŌĢóčŚ5.5, not from each other). Record the cross-edges explicitly in each chunk PR.
- `registry.ts` imports `context.ts` and every `handlers/*`. It exports `SKILL_HANDLERS` and the `skillExecutor` object (the `{ execute }` closure that dispatches by slug, handles the `mcp.*` prefix branch, and stashes `toolCallId` on the context ąō?" exactly the body of `skillExecutor.execute` today). The private `SkillExecutionParams` interface stays here, next to `execute`. No other logic ąō?" the ŌĢóčŚ5.3 rule is "assembly + execute closure only".
- `adapter-registration.ts` imports `context.ts` (for `SkillExecutionContext`), `executionLayerService` (`registerAdapter`), `adapters/workerAdapter` (`createWorkerAdapter`), `config/actionRegistry` (`resolveActionSlug`), the per-action approved executors from `handlers/delegation.ts`, and the page executors from `handlers/pages.ts` (`executeCreatePage`/`executeUpdatePage`/`executePublishPage` ąō?" the worker dispatch routes these three slugs to non-`*Approved` handlers in the page family). Two slugs use dynamic `await import(...)` inside the dispatch and stay as such: `config_update_organisation_config` (imports `configUpdateOrganisationService.executeApprovedOrganisationConfigUpdate`) and `notify_operator` (imports `notifyOperatorFanoutService.fanoutOperatorAlert`). Adapter-registration MAY NOT import the barrel `skillExecutor.ts` and MAY NOT import any other `handlers/*` module beyond the two named above.
- The barrel imports `adapter-registration.ts` for its side effect (worker adapter registration MUST happen exactly once at barrel load).
- No file under `skillExecutor/` may import the barrel `skillExecutor.ts`. If it needs the public `skillExecutor` object, it imports `skillExecutor/registry.ts` and constructs `{ execute }` itself ąō?" which is exactly what the barrel does.

### 5.4. Pure / impure separation rules

Per `DEVELOPMENT_GUIDELINES.md ŌĢóčŚ2`: pure helpers live in `lib/`, not `services/`. The existing `skillExecutorPure.ts` and `skillExecutorDelegationPure.ts` are tolerated exceptions because they were extracted from a service and stay co-located for grepability.

Convention going forward: when a chunk of a `handlers/*` module is pure (no DB, no env, no service imports, no I/O), extract it to a `<topic>Pure.ts` sibling under `skillExecutor/` and import it from the handler. Examples that already exist:
- `skillExecutorPure.ts` ąō?" `applyOnFailurePure`, `applyOnFailureForStructuredFailurePure`, `OnFailureDirective`
- `skillExecutorDelegationPure.ts` ąō?" `resolveWriteSkillScope`, `classifySpawnTargets`, `computeReassignDirection`, etc.

This build does NOT proactively hunt for new Pure extractions. It only acknowledges the rule so future audits and edits know where to put new pure helpers.

### 5.5. Module-level state rules

Two module-level state sites exist today in `skillExecutor.ts`:
1. `processorRegistry: Map<string, ProcessorHooks>` ąō?" lives in `pipeline.ts` after the split. `registerProcessor` and `runWithProcessors` are the only readers/writers.
2. `pgBossSend: ((name, data) => Promise<string | null>) | null` ąō?" set by `setHandoffJobSender`, read by `enqueueHandoff`. Both live in `pipeline.ts`. Handlers that need to enqueue a handoff (currently `executeReassignTask` and `executeSpawnSubAgents`) import `enqueueHandoff` from `pipeline.ts`.

NO new module-level state introduced. NO existing module-level state duplicated across sub-modules.

### 5.6. Test-collocation rule

For every handler family that has a co-located test (`__tests__/<topic>.test.ts`), the test stays at its current path. Imports inside the test file may be updated to point at the new handler location, but the test file's location is NOT changed in this build.

`__tests__/skillHandlerRegistryEquivalence.test.ts` is the registry contract test ąō?" it enumerates `SKILL_HANDLERS` and asserts the slug set matches the registered action types (or whatever invariant it pins). Its assertions stay identical; only the import path of `SKILL_HANDLERS` may change (and even that stays the same if the barrel preserves the export, which is the default).

### 5.7. Barrel re-export shape

```typescript
// server/services/skillExecutor.ts (target shape)
import './skillExecutor/adapter-registration.js';  // side-effect import
export { skillExecutor, SKILL_HANDLERS } from './skillExecutor/registry.js';
export type { SkillExecutionContext, SkillHandler } from './skillExecutor/context.js';
export { registerProcessor, setHandoffJobSender } from './skillExecutor/pipeline.js';
```

The `skillExecutor` constant `{ execute }` lives in `registry.ts` so it closes over `SKILL_HANDLERS` in the same module. The private `SkillExecutionParams` interface (the argument shape of `execute`) stays in `registry.ts` next to its only consumer. The architect plan may revisit if there's a strong reason to put `skillExecutor` in the barrel; default is `registry.ts`.

221:   * (list_platform_capabilities, list_connections, check_capability_gap).
222:   * Enforced against systemSettings.orchestrator_capability_query_budget
223:   * (default 8). When exhausted, further calls return
224:   * { error: 'capability_query_budget_exhausted' } so the Orchestrator
225:   * stops looping rather than burning tokens. See
226:   * docs/orchestrator-capability-routing-spec.md ┬¦6.4.3.
227:   */
228:  capabilityQueryCallCount?: number;
229:}
230:
231:interface SkillExecutionParams {
232:  skillName: string;
233:  input: Record<string, unknown>;
234:  context: SkillExecutionContext;
235:  /**
236:   * Tool call ID from the LLM response. Sprint 2 P1.1 Layer 3 requires a
237:   * deterministic idempotency key so the proposeActionMiddleware and the
238:   * per-case action wrappers both resolve to the same action row. When
239:   * omitted (legacy callers), the wrappers fall back to a non-deterministic
240:   * key. The middleware + wrapper coexistence relies on this being set.
241:   */
242:  toolCallId?: string;
243:}
244:
245:/**
246: * Asserts that the skill execution context has a subaccountId.
247: * Call this at the top of any skill that requires subaccount scope.
248: * Returns the subaccountId as a non-null string for downstream use.
249: */
250:function requireSubaccountContext(context: SkillExecutionContext, skillName: string): string {
251:  if (!context.subaccountId) {
252:    throw new Error(`Skill '${skillName}' requires a subaccount context but this is an org-level run. Use a subaccount-scoped agent or specify a targetSubaccountId.`);
253:  }
254:  return context.subaccountId;
255:}
256:
257:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
258:// onFailure dispatch (P0.2 Slice C of docs/improvements-roadmap-spec.md)
259://
260:// When a skill handler throws or returns { success: false, ... }, look up
261:// the action definition's `onFailure` directive and dispatch:
262://
263://   - 'retry' (default)  ŌĆö propagate the original error / failure object
264://                          unchanged. Caller is responsible for retry logic
265://                          (withBackoff / TripWire / agent loop).
266://   - 'skip'             ŌĆö return { success: false, skipped: true, reason }
267://                          to the LLM. The agent loop continues without the
268://                          result. Used for non-essential reads.
269://   - 'fail_run'         ŌĆö terminate the entire agent run via the closed
270://                          FailureReason enum. Caller catches via FailureError.
271://   - 'fallback'         ŌĆö return actionDef.fallbackValue as the result
272://                          instead of failing. Used for read-only tools where
273://                          a stale or empty value is preferable.
274:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
275:
276:import {
277:  applyOnFailurePure,
278:  applyOnFailureForStructuredFailurePure,
279:  type OnFailureDirective,
280:} from './skillExecutorPure.js';
281:
282:function applyOnFailure(toolSlug: string, err: unknown): unknown {
283:  const actionDef = getActionDefinition(toolSlug);
284:  const directive: OnFailureDirective = actionDef?.onFailure ?? 'retry';
285:  return applyOnFailurePure(toolSlug, directive, actionDef?.fallbackValue, err);
286:}
287:
288:function applyOnFailureForStructuredFailure(
289:  toolSlug: string,
290:  result: Record<string, unknown>,
291:): unknown {
292:  const actionDef = getActionDefinition(toolSlug);
293:  const directive: OnFailureDirective = actionDef?.onFailure ?? 'retry';
294:  return applyOnFailureForStructuredFailurePure(toolSlug, directive, actionDef?.fallbackValue, result);
295:}
296:
297:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
298:// Per-tool processor hooks registry
299:// Maps action type slug ŌåÆ ProcessorHooks (input/output transform pipeline)
300:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
301:
302:const processorRegistry: Map<string, ProcessorHooks> = new Map();
303:
304:/** Register processor hooks for a tool slug. Called at module load time. */
305:export function registerProcessor(toolSlug: string, hooks: ProcessorHooks): void {
306:  processorRegistry.set(toolSlug, hooks);
307:}
308:
309:/** Internal: run registered processor phases around a tool executor. */
310:async function runWithProcessors(
311:  toolSlug: string,
312:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
313:  context: SkillExecutionContext,
314:  executor: (processedInput: Record<string, unknown>) => Promise<unknown>,
315:  actionId?: string,
316:): Promise<unknown> {
317:  const hooks = processorRegistry.get(toolSlug);
318:  const processorCtx: ProcessorContext = {
319:    toolSlug,
320:    input,
321:    subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
322:    organisationId: context.organisationId,
323:    agentRunId: context.runId,
324:    actionId,
325:  };
326:
327:  let processedInput = input;
328:
329:  // Phase 1: processInput (before gate)
330:  if (hooks?.processInput) {
331:    try {
332:      processedInput = (await hooks.processInput({ ...processorCtx, input: processedInput })) as Record<string, unknown>;
333:    } catch (err) {
334:      if (err instanceof TripWire) {
335:        if (!err.options.retry) throw err;  // fatal ŌĆö propagate to caller
336:        return { success: false, error: err.reason, retryable: true };
337:      }
338:      throw err;
339:    }
340:  }
341:
342:  // Phase 2: processInputStep (after gate, before execute)
343:  if (hooks?.processInputStep) {
344:    try {
345:      processedInput = (await hooks.processInputStep({ ...processorCtx, input: processedInput })) as Record<string, unknown>;
346:    } catch (err) {
347:      if (err instanceof TripWire) {
348:        if (!err.options.retry) throw err;
349:        return { success: false, error: err.reason, retryable: true };
350:      }
351:      throw err;
352:    }
353:  }
354:
355:  // Execute ŌĆö dispatch on actionDef.onFailure (P0.2 Slice C) for failures.
356:  let result: unknown;
357:  try {
358:    result = await executor(processedInput);
359:  } catch (err) {
360:    if (err instanceof TripWire) {
361:      return { success: false, error: err.reason, retryable: err.options.retry };
362:    }
363:    // Non-TripWire failure ŌĆö apply the action's onFailure directive if declared.
364:    // When fail_run fires, record a system incident before propagating.
365:    const actionDef = getActionDefinition(toolSlug);
366:    if ((actionDef?.onFailure ?? 'retry') === 'fail_run') {
367:      recordIncident({
368:        source: 'skill',
369:        summary: `Skill terminal failure: ${toolSlug} ŌĆö ${err instanceof Error ? err.message.slice(0, 200) : String(err)}`,
370:        errorCode: 'skill_fail_run',
371:        stack: err instanceof Error ? err.stack : undefined,
372:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
373:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
374:        fingerprintOverride: `skill:${toolSlug}:fail_run`,
375:      });
376:    }
377:    return applyOnFailure(toolSlug, err);
378:  }
379:
380:  // Successful return value but the executor signalled a structured failure.
381:  // Apply onFailure here too so 'skip' / 'fallback' fire on either error path.
382:  if (
383:    result !== null &&
384:    typeof result === 'object' &&
385:    (result as { success?: unknown }).success === false
386:  ) {
387:    // Symmetric with the thrown-error path: the pure helper already handles
388:    // 'retry' / unset by returning the result unchanged.
389:    result = applyOnFailureForStructuredFailure(toolSlug, result as Record<string, unknown>);
390:  }
391:
392:  // Phase 3: processOutputStep (after execute)
393:  if (hooks?.processOutputStep) {
394:    try {
395:      result = await hooks.processOutputStep({ ...processorCtx, input: processedInput, actionId }, result);
396:    } catch (err) {
397:      if (err instanceof TripWire) {
398:        if (!err.options.retry) throw err;
399:        return { success: false, error: err.reason, retryable: true };
400:      }
401:      throw err;
402:    }
403:  }
404:
405:  return result;
406:}
407:
408:// Handoff job queue name
409:const AGENT_HANDOFF_QUEUE = 'agent-handoff-run';
410:
411:// pg-boss reference for enqueueing handoff jobs (set by agentScheduleService)
412:let pgBossSend: ((name: string, data: object) => Promise<string | null>) | null = null;
413:
414:export function setHandoffJobSender(sender: (name: string, data: object) => Promise<string | null>) {
415:  pgBossSend = sender;
416:}
417:
418:/**
419: * Signature for a skill handler entry in SKILL_HANDLERS. Each entry is an
420: * async function that receives the raw tool input and the current skill
421: * execution context and returns whatever value the LLM should observe as the
422: * tool result. This is the Phase 0 replacement for the old switch statement
423: * dispatch ŌĆö keeping the registry shape explicit (not a Map) so static
424: * analysis and the skill-analyzer can walk the keys directly.
425: */
426:export type SkillHandler = (
427:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
428:  context: SkillExecutionContext,
429:) => Promise<unknown>;
430:
431:/**
432: * Registry of skill handlers keyed by skill name. The `skillExecutor.execute`
433: * method dispatches to an entry here after handling the MCP prefix and the
434: * toolCallId stash. Previously this was a 770-line switch statement; it now
435: * lives as a module-level constant so other modules (notably the
436: * skill-analyzer) can enumerate the supported skill names without having to
437: * parse source code.

466:        query: input.query as string,

470:        topK: (input.topK as number) ?? 10,

489:        { limit: (input.limit as number) ?? 20 },
490:      );
491:      return { success: true, items };
492:    } else if (op === 'claim') {

494:        input.source as string,

496:        context.runId,

498:      );
499:      return { success: result.claimed, ...result };
500:    } else if (op === 'release') {

502:        input.source as string,
503:        input.itemId as string,
504:        context.runId,
505:      );

1436:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ CRM Query Planner (read-only, not review-gated) ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
1437:  // Agent-facing tool per spec ┬¦18.2 ŌĆö dispatches through the planner
1438:  // pipeline (Stage 1 registry / Stage 2 cache / Stage 3 LLM fallback /
1439:  // canonical + live + hybrid executors) and returns the BriefResultContract
1440:  // artefact set. The route at /api/crm-query-planner/query is the user
1441:  // surface; this handler is the agent surface.
1442:  'crm.query': async (input, context) => {
1443:    // Resolve target subaccount ŌĆö prefer the explicit tool-input value,
1444:    // falling back to the agent's bound subaccount context.
1445:    const suppliedSubaccountId = typeof input.subaccountId === 'string' && input.subaccountId.length > 0
1446:      ? input.subaccountId
1447:      : null;
1448:    const targetSubaccountId = suppliedSubaccountId ?? context.subaccountId;
1449:
1450:    if (!targetSubaccountId) {
1451:      return {
1452:        success: false,
1453:        error:   'missing_permission',
1454:        message: 'crm.query requires a subaccount ŌĆö supply input.subaccountId or bind the agent to a subaccount.',
1455:      };
1456:    }
1457:
1458:    // Horizontal-access guard (mirrors intelligenceSkillExecutor.executeQuerySubaccountCohort):
1459:    // a regular subaccount agent may only read its own subaccount. Only
1460:    // org-subaccount agents (allowedSubaccountIds === null) may cross
1461:    // boundaries, and even then only to subaccounts in their allowlist if
1462:    // the array form is present. Skip when the caller made no explicit
1463:    // cross-subaccount request (input.subaccountId matches context or was omitted).
1464:    if (suppliedSubaccountId && suppliedSubaccountId !== context.subaccountId) {
1465:      const allowed = context.allowedSubaccountIds;
1466:      const isOrgScope = allowed === null || allowed === undefined;
1467:      const inAllowlist = Array.isArray(allowed) && allowed.includes(suppliedSubaccountId);
1468:      if (!isOrgScope && !inAllowlist) {
1469:        return {
1470:          success: false,
1471:          error:   'missing_permission',
1472:          message: 'Agent is not authorised to read the specified subaccount.',
1473:        };
1474:      }
1475:    }
1476:
1477:    const { runQuery } = await import('./crmQueryPlanner/index.js');
1478:    const result = await runQuery(
1479:      {
1480:        rawIntent:    String(input.rawIntent ?? ''),
1481:        subaccountId: targetSubaccountId,
1482:        briefId:      typeof input.briefId === 'string' ? input.briefId : undefined,
1483:      },
1484:      {
1485:        orgId:                  context.organisationId,
1486:        organisationId:         context.organisationId,
1487:        subaccountId:           targetSubaccountId,
1488:        runId:                  context.runId,
1489:        briefId:                typeof input.briefId === 'string' ? input.briefId : undefined,
1490:        principalType:          'agent',
1491:        principalId:            context.agentId,
1492:        teamIds:                [],
1493:        // Agent-invoked ŌĆö the agent's own capabilityMap gated the skill
1494:        // dispatch upstream (skillExecutor.execute). The planner's
1495:        // validator treats unknown `canonical.*` slugs as skipped per
1496:        // ┬¦12.1, so the route's subaccount-capability union is not
1497:        // required here ŌĆö `crm.query` is the only hard-gated slug.
1498:        callerCapabilities:     new Set<string>(['crm.query']),
1499:        defaultSenderIdentifier: undefined,
1500:      },
1501:    );
1502:    return { success: true, ...result };
1503:  },
1504:

1643:      subaccountId,
1644:      organisationId,
1645:      artefactTitle,
1646:      artefactContent,
1647:      deliveryChannels,
1648:    } = input as Record<string, unknown>;
1649:
1650:    if (!subaccountId || !organisationId || !artefactTitle || !artefactContent) {
1651:      return { success: false, error: 'subaccountId, organisationId, artefactTitle, artefactContent required' };
1652:    }

1655:      (deliveryChannels as { email?: boolean; portal?: boolean; slack?: boolean } | undefined) ??
1656:      { email: true, portal: true, slack: false };

1659:      {
1660:        title: String(artefactTitle),
1661:        content: String(artefactContent),
1662:        createdByAgentId: context.agentId,
1663:      },
1664:      {
1665:        email: Boolean(config.email ?? true),
1666:        portal: Boolean(config.portal ?? true),
1667:        slack: Boolean(config.slack ?? false),
1668:      },
1669:      String(subaccountId),
1670:      String(organisationId),
1671:    );
1672:
1673:    return {
1674:      success: true,
1675:      taskId: result.taskId,
1676:      channels: result.channels,
1677:    };

1903:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ Sub-Account Optimiser: generic agent-output primitive (Chunk 1) ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
1904:  // output.recommend ŌĆö any agent with this skill can surface operator-facing
1905:  // recommendations via the generic agent_recommendations primitive.
1906:  // Spec: docs/sub-account-optimiser-spec.md ┬¦6.2
1907:  'output.recommend': async (input, context) => {
1908:    // Requires an agent execution context ŌĆö non-agent callers are rejected.
1909:    if (!context.agentId) {
1910:      return {
1911:        success: false,
1912:        error: 'output.recommend requires an agent execution context (agentId missing)',
1913:      };
1914:    }
1915:
1916:    const {
1917:      scope_type,
1918:      scope_id,
1919:      category,
1920:      severity,
1921:      title,
1922:      body,
1923:      evidence,
1924:      action_hint,
1925:      dedupe_key,
1926:    } = input as Record<string, unknown>;
1927:
1928:    // Validate required fields
1929:    if (!scope_type || (scope_type !== 'org' && scope_type !== 'subaccount')) {
1930:      return { success: false, error: 'scope_type must be "org" or "subaccount"' };
1931:    }
1932:    if (!scope_id || typeof scope_id !== 'string') {
1933:      return { success: false, error: 'scope_id must be a valid UUID string' };
1934:    }
1935:    // Basic UUID validation
1936:    const uuidRegex = /^[0-9a-f]{8}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{4}-[0-9a-f]{12}$/i;
1937:    if (!uuidRegex.test(scope_id)) {
1938:      return { success: false, error: 'scope_id must be a valid UUID' };
1939:    }
1940:    if (!severity || !['info', 'warn', 'critical'].includes(severity as string)) {
1941:      return { success: false, error: 'severity must be "info", "warn", or "critical"' };
1942:    }
1943:    if (!category || typeof category !== 'string') {
1944:      return { success: false, error: 'category is required' };
1945:    }
1946:    // Validate three-segment format
1947:    const categoryParts = (category as string).split('.');
1948:    if (categoryParts.length < 3) {
1949:      return {
1950:        success: false,
1951:        error: 'category must follow <agent_namespace>.<area>.<finding> format (three segments)',
1952:      };
1953:    }
1954:    if (!title || typeof title !== 'string') {
1955:      return { success: false, error: 'title is required' };
1956:    }
1957:    if (!body || typeof body !== 'string') {
1958:      return { success: false, error: 'body is required' };
1959:    }
1960:    if (!evidence || typeof evidence !== 'object' || Array.isArray(evidence)) {
1961:      return { success: false, error: 'evidence must be a plain object' };
1962:    }
1963:    if (!dedupe_key || typeof dedupe_key !== 'string') {
1964:      return { success: false, error: 'dedupe_key is required' };
1965:    }
1966:    // Validate action_hint: null/omitted accepted; non-null must match scheme://path format
1967:    if (action_hint !== undefined && action_hint !== null) {
1968:      if (typeof action_hint !== 'string' || action_hint === '') {
1969:        return { success: false, error: 'action_hint must be null/omitted or a non-empty URI string' };
1970:      }
1971:      const actionHintRegex = /^[a-z][a-z0-9-]*:\/\/[^\s]+$/;
1972:      if (!actionHintRegex.test(action_hint as string)) {
1973:        return {
1974:          success: false,
1975:          error: 'action_hint must match pattern ^[a-z][a-z0-9-]*://[^\\s]+$ (e.g. configuration-assistant://agent/id?focus=budget)',
1976:        };
1977:      }
1978:    }
1979:
1980:    const { upsertRecommendation } = await import('./agentRecommendationsService.js');
1981:    const result = await upsertRecommendation(
1982:      {
1983:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
1984:        agentId: context.agentId,
1985:      },
1986:      {
1987:        scope_type: scope_type as 'org' | 'subaccount',
1988:        scope_id: scope_id as string,
1989:        category: category as string,
1990:        severity: severity as 'info' | 'warn' | 'critical',
1991:        title: title as string,
1992:        body: body as string,
1993:        evidence: evidence as Record<string, unknown>,
1994:        action_hint: (action_hint as string | null | undefined) ?? null,
1995:        dedupe_key: dedupe_key as string,
1996:      },
1997:    );
1998:    return { success: true, ...result };
1999:  },

2323:    if (contacts.length === 0) return { success: true, contacts: [], tickets: [], revenue: [], accounts: [] };
2324:    const contactIds = contacts.map((c) => c.id);
2325:    const accountIds = [...new Set(contacts.map((c) => c.accountId))];
2326:    const tickets = await db
2327:      .select()
2328:      .from(ctTickets)
2329:      .where(and(
2330:        eq(ctTickets.organisationId, context.organisationId),
2331:        inArr(ctTickets.canonicalContactId, contactIds),
2332:      ))
2333:      .orderBy(ctTickets.openedAt);
2334:    const revenue = await db
2335:      .select()
2336:      .from(canonicalRevenue) // verify-canonical-read-interface: allowed
2337:      .where(and(
2338:        eq(canonicalRevenue.organisationId, context.organisationId), // verify-canonical-read-interface: allowed
2339:        inArr(canonicalRevenue.accountId, accountIds), // verify-canonical-read-interface: allowed
2340:      ));
2341:    const accounts = await db
2342:      .select()
2343:      .from(canonicalAccounts) // verify-canonical-read-interface: allowed
2344:      .where(and(
2345:        eq(canonicalAccounts.organisationId, context.organisationId), // verify-canonical-read-interface: allowed
2346:        inArr(canonicalAccounts.id, accountIds), // verify-canonical-read-interface: allowed
2347:      ));
2348:    return { success: true, contacts, tickets, revenue, accounts };
2349:  },
2350:} satisfies Record<string, SkillHandler>);

2356:async function resolveAgentOwner(context: SkillExecutionContext): Promise<string> {
2357:  const { db: agentDb } = await import('../db/index.js');
2358:  const { agents: agentsTable } = await import('../db/schema/agents.js');
2359:  const { eq: eqOp } = await import('drizzle-orm');
2360:  const [agent] = await agentDb
2361:    .select({ ownerUserId: agentsTable.ownerUserId })
2362:    .from(agentsTable)
2363:    .where(eqOp(agentsTable.id, context.agentId))
2364:    .limit(1);
2365:  if (!agent?.ownerUserId) {
2366:    throw Object.assign(
2367:      new Error('Agent has no owner; this skill requires a user-owned agent'),
2368:      { statusCode: 422, errorCode: 'AGENT_NO_OWNER' },
2369:    );
2370:  }
2371:  return agent.ownerUserId;
2372:}

2495:export const skillExecutor = {
2496:  async execute(params: SkillExecutionParams): Promise<unknown> {
2497:    const { skillName, input, context, toolCallId } = params;
2498:    // Stash the current tool call id on the context so the per-case
2499:    // action wrappers below can build the same deterministic idempotency
2500:    // key that proposeActionMiddleware wrote for this call (Sprint 2 P1.1
2501:    // Layer 3). Mutation is safe ŌĆö the context is scoped to one run and
2502:    // one tool call at a time.
2503:    if (toolCallId !== undefined) {
2504:      context.toolCallId = toolCallId;
2505:    }
2506:
2507:    // MCP tool dispatch ŌĆö tool slugs start with "mcp."
2508:    if (skillName.startsWith('mcp.') && context._mcpClients) {
2509:      const { mcpClientManager } = await import('./mcpClientManager.js');
2510:      return mcpClientManager.callTool(
2511:        context._mcpClients,
2512:        context._mcpLazyRegistry ?? new Map(),
2513:        skillName,
2514:        input,
2515:        {
2516:          runId: context.runId,
2517:          organisationId: context.organisationId,
2518:          agentId: context.agentId,
2519:          subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
2520:          isTestRun: context.isTestRun ?? false,
2521:          taskId: context.taskId,
2522:          mcpCallCount: context.mcpCallCount,
2523:        },
2524:      );
2525:    }
2526:
2527:    const handler = SKILL_HANDLERS[skillName];
2528:    if (!handler) {
2529:      return { success: false, error: `Unknown skill: ${skillName}` };
2530:    }
2531:    return handler(input, context);
2532:  },
2533:};
2534:
2535:
2536:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2537:// Action-gated execution helpers
2538:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2539:
2540:/**
2541: * Wraps an auto-gated internal skill: creates an action record for auditability,
2542: * executes synchronously, and records the result.
2543: *
2544: * If the policy engine has escalated this skill to review (returns pending_approval),
2545: * we fall through to the review-gate path so the agent still gets a proper result.
2546: */
2547:async function executeWithActionAudit(
2548:  actionType: string,
2549:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
2550:  context: SkillExecutionContext,
2551:  executor: () => Promise<unknown>
2552:): Promise<unknown> {
2553:  // Sprint 2 P1.1 Layer 3: when a toolCallId is on the context, build a
2554:  // deterministic key that matches the one proposeActionMiddleware already
2555:  // wrote for this call. proposeAction() short-circuits on the existing
2556:  // row (isNew === false) and the wrapper moves on to execution. Legacy
2557:  // callers without a toolCallId fall back to the old timestamp key.
2558:  const idempotencyKey = context.toolCallId
2559:    ? buildActionIdempotencyKey({
2560:        runId: context.runId,
2561:        toolCallId: context.toolCallId,
2562:        args: input,
2563:      })
2564:    : `${actionType}:${context.runId}:${Date.now()}`;
2565:  const pipelineSpan = createSpan('skill.pipeline.run', { skillName: actionType, gateLevel: 'auto' }, { input });
2566:
2567:  try {
2568:    const proposed = await actionService.proposeAction({
2569:      organisationId: context.organisationId,
2570:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
2571:      agentId: context.agentId,
2572:      agentRunId: context.runId,
2573:      actionType,
2574:      idempotencyKey,
2575:      payload: input,
2576:      taskId: context.taskId,
2577:    });
2578:
2579:    createEvent('skill.action.proposed', {
2580:      skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId, status: proposed.status,
2581:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2582:
2583:    // Duplicate detected ŌĆö return existing status
2584:    if (!proposed.isNew) {
2585:      const dupeResult = { success: true, action_id: proposed.actionId, status: proposed.status, message: 'Duplicate action detected' };
2586:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: dupeResult });
2587:      return dupeResult;
2588:    }
2589:
2590:    // Policy engine escalated to block ŌĆö return denial immediately
2591:    if (proposed.status === 'blocked') {
2592:      createEvent('skill.gate.decision', {
2593:        gateLevel: 'block', skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId,
2594:      }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2595:      const denial = buildDenialMessage(actionType, 'This action is blocked by policy for this account.');
2596:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: denial });
2597:      return denial;
2598:    }
2599:
2600:    // Policy engine escalated to review ŌĆö block and await human decision
2601:    if (proposed.status === 'pending_approval') {
2602:      createEvent('skill.gate.decision', {
2603:        gateLevel: 'review', skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId,
2604:      }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2605:      const action = await actionService.getAction(proposed.actionId, context.organisationId);
2606:      await reviewService.createReviewItem(action, {
2607:        actionType,
2608:        reasoning: input.metadata ? String((input.metadata as Record<string, unknown>).reasoning ?? '') : undefined,
2609:        proposedPayload: input,
2610:      });
2611:      const reviewResult = await awaitReviewDecision(proposed.actionId, actionType, context);
2612:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: reviewResult });
2613:      return reviewResult;
2614:    }
2615:
2616:    createEvent('skill.gate.decision', {
2617:      gateLevel: 'auto', skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId,
2618:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2619:
2620:    // Auto-approved ŌĆö execute inline with processor pipeline
2621:    const locked = await actionService.lockForExecution(proposed.actionId, context.organisationId);
2622:    if (!locked) {
2623:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: { success: false, error: 'Failed to acquire execution lock' } });
2624:      return { success: false, error: 'Failed to acquire execution lock' };
2625:    }
2626:
2627:    const executeSpan = createSpan('skill.phase.execute', { skillName: actionType }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2628:    const result = await runWithProcessors(
2629:      actionType,
2630:      input,
2631:      context,
2632:      (_processedInput) => executor(),
2633:      proposed.actionId,
2634:    );
2635:    executeSpan.end({ output: result });
2636:
2637:    const resultObj = result as Record<string, unknown>;
2638:    if (resultObj?.success) {
2639:      await actionService.markCompleted(proposed.actionId, context.organisationId, result);
2640:    } else {
2641:      await actionService.markFailed(proposed.actionId, context.organisationId, String(resultObj?.error ?? 'Unknown error'));
2642:    }
2643:
2644:    pipelineSpan.end({ output: result });
2645:    return result;
2646:  } catch (err) {
2647:    if (err instanceof TripWire && !err.options.retry) {
2648:      createEvent('skill.tripwire.triggered', {
2649:        skillName: actionType, fatal: true, reason: err.reason, code: err.options.code,
2650:      }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan, level: 'ERROR' });
2651:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: { success: false, error: err.reason } });
2652:      return { success: false, error: `Action halted: ${err.reason}`, code: err.options.code };
2653:    }
2654:    createEvent('skill.action.failed', {
2655:      skillName: actionType, error: String(err).slice(0, 200),
2656:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan, level: 'ERROR' });
2657:    console.error(`[ActionAudit] Failed to track ${actionType}, executing directly:`, err);
2658:    pipelineSpan.end({ output: { error: String(err) } });
2659:    return executor();
2660:  }
2661:}
2662:
2663:/**
2664: * Proposes a review-gated action and BLOCKS until a human decides.
2665: *
2666: * Returns:
2667: *   - On approval: the execution result from the adapter (via hitlService)
2668: *   - On rejection/timeout: a structured denial observation (not an exception)
2669: *
2670: * The agent receives this as a normal tool call result and continues its loop.
2671: */
2672:async function proposeReviewGatedAction(
2673:  actionType: string,
2674:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
2675:  context: SkillExecutionContext
2676:): Promise<unknown> {
2677:  const definition = getActionDefinition(actionType);
2678:  if (!definition) {
2679:    return { success: false, error: `Unknown action type: ${actionType}` };
2680:  }
2681:
2682:  const pipelineSpan = createSpan('skill.pipeline.run', { skillName: actionType, gateLevel: 'review' }, { input });
2683:
2684:  // Sprint 2 P1.1 Layer 3: deterministic key matches the middleware's so
2685:  // both paths resolve to the same action row. Legacy fallback preserves
2686:  // the old per-field key for callers that still lack a toolCallId.
2687:  let idempotencyKey: string;
2688:  if (context.toolCallId) {
2689:    idempotencyKey = buildActionIdempotencyKey({
2690:      runId: context.runId,
2691:      toolCallId: context.toolCallId,
2692:      args: input,
2693:    });
2694:  } else {
2695:    const keyParts = [actionType, context.subaccountId ?? `org:${context.organisationId}`];
2696:    if (input.thread_id) keyParts.push(String(input.thread_id));
2697:    if (input.record_id) keyParts.push(String(input.record_id));
2698:    keyParts.push(String(Date.now()));
2699:    idempotencyKey = keyParts.join(':');
2700:  }
2701:
2702:  try {
2703:    const proposed = await actionService.proposeAction({
2704:      organisationId: context.organisationId,
2705:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
2706:      agentId: context.agentId,
2707:      agentRunId: context.runId,
2708:      actionType,
2709:      idempotencyKey,
2710:      payload: input,
2711:      metadata: input.metadata as Record<string, unknown> | undefined,
2712:      taskId: context.taskId,
2713:    });
2714:
2715:    createEvent('skill.action.proposed', {
2716:      skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId, status: proposed.status,
2717:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2718:
2719:    // Duplicate ŌĆö return its current status
2720:    if (!proposed.isNew) {
2721:      const result = { success: true, action_id: proposed.actionId, status: proposed.status, message: 'Action already exists (duplicate detected)' };
2722:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: result });
2723:      return result;
2724:    }
2725:
2726:    // Policy engine blocked it ŌĆö return denial immediately, no review queue entry
2727:    if (proposed.status === 'blocked') {
2728:      createEvent('skill.gate.decision', {
2729:        gateLevel: 'block', skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId,
2730:      }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2731:      const denial = buildDenialMessage(actionType, 'This action is blocked by policy for this account.');
2732:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: denial });
2733:      return denial;
2734:    }
2735:
2736:    // Policy engine auto-approved it ŌĆö should not happen for review-gated skills,
2737:    // but handle it gracefully by dispatching immediately
2738:    if (proposed.status === 'approved') {
2739:      createEvent('skill.gate.decision', {
2740:        gateLevel: 'auto', skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId,
2741:      }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2742:      await executionLayerService.executeAction(proposed.actionId, context.organisationId);
2743:      const result = { success: true, action_id: proposed.actionId, status: 'completed', message: 'Action auto-approved and executed.' };
2744:      pipelineSpan.end({ output: result });
2745:      return result;
2746:    }
2747:
2748:    createEvent('skill.gate.decision', {
2749:      gateLevel: 'review', skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId,
2750:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2751:
2752:    // pending_approval ŌĆö create review item, then block until decision
2753:    const action = await actionService.getAction(proposed.actionId, context.organisationId);
2754:    await reviewService.createReviewItem(action, {
2755:      actionType,
2756:      reasoning: input.metadata ? String((input.metadata as Record<string, unknown>).reasoning ?? '') : undefined,
2757:      proposedPayload: input,
2758:    });
2759:
2760:    const reviewStartTime = Date.now();
2761:    const reviewSpan = createSpan('skill.review.wait', {
2762:      skillName: actionType, actionId: proposed.actionId, criticalPath: true,
2763:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan });
2764:
2765:    const reviewResult = await awaitReviewDecision(proposed.actionId, actionType, context);
2766:
2767:    reviewSpan.end({
2768:      output: {
2769:        approved: !!(reviewResult && typeof reviewResult === 'object' && (reviewResult as Record<string, unknown>).success),
2770:        waitDurationMs: Date.now() - reviewStartTime,
2771:      },
2772:    });
2773:    pipelineSpan.end({ output: reviewResult });
2774:    return reviewResult;
2775:  } catch (err) {
2776:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
2777:    createEvent('skill.action.failed', {
2778:      skillName: actionType, error: errMsg.slice(0, 200),
2779:    }, { parentSpan: pipelineSpan, level: 'ERROR' });
2780:    pipelineSpan.end({ output: { success: false, error: errMsg } });
2781:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to propose ${actionType}: ${errMsg}` };
2782:  }
2783:}
2784:
2785:/**
2786: * Shared await logic: blocks until hitlService resolves the decision,
2787: * then returns the execution result or a denial observation.
2788: */
2789:async function awaitReviewDecision(
2790:  actionId: string,
2791:  actionType: string,
2792:  context: SkillExecutionContext
2793:): Promise<unknown> {
2794:  const decision = await hitlService.awaitDecision(actionId, HITL_REVIEW_TIMEOUT_MS);
2795:
2796:  if (!decision.approved) {
2797:    return buildDenialMessage(actionType, decision.comment ?? 'No reason provided');
2798:  }
2799:
2800:  // Return the execution result that reviewService ran via executionLayerService
2801:  return {
2802:    success: true,
2803:    action_id: actionId,
2804:    status: 'completed',
2805:    result: decision.result,
2806:    edited: decision.editedArgs ? true : undefined,
2807:  };
2808:}
2809:
2810:/**
2811: * Builds a structured denial observation that the agent receives as a tool result.
2812: * The agent continues its loop ŌĆö this is never thrown as an exception.
2813: * Pattern from n8n: inject the denial as a tool output, not an error.
2814: */
2815:function buildDenialMessage(actionType: string, comment: string): Record<string, unknown> {
2816:  return {
2817:    success: false,
2818:    status: 'denied',
2819:    action_type: actionType,
2820:    message: `Action '${actionType}' was not approved. Reason: ${comment}`,
2821:    instruction: 'Do not retry this action automatically. Inform the user or adjust your approach based on the feedback.',
2822:  };
2823:}
2824:
2825:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2826:// Web Search (Tavily)
2827:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2828:
2829:async function executeWebSearch(input: Record<string, unknown>, context: SkillExecutionContext): Promise<unknown> {
2830:  const apiKey = env.TAVILY_API_KEY;
2831:  if (!apiKey) {
2832:    return { success: false, error: 'Web search is not configured (TAVILY_API_KEY not set)' };
2833:  }
2834:
2835:  const query = String(input.query ?? '');
2836:  const maxResults = Math.min(Number(input.max_results ?? 5), 10);
2837:
2838:  try {
2839:    const response = await fetch('https://api.tavily.com/search', {
2840:      method: 'POST',
2841:      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
2842:      body: JSON.stringify({
2843:        api_key: apiKey,
2844:        query,
2845:        max_results: maxResults,
2846:        include_answer: true,
2847:        include_raw_content: false,
2848:      }),
2849:      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(15_000),
2850:    });
2851:
2852:    if (!response.ok) {
2853:      const errorText = await response.text().catch(() => response.statusText);
2854:      return { success: false, error: `Search API error: ${errorText}` };
2855:    }
2856:
2857:    const data = await response.json() as {
2858:      answer?: string;
2859:      results?: Array<{
2860:        title: string;
2861:        url: string;
2862:        content: string;
2863:        score: number;
2864:      }>;
2865:    };
2866:
2867:    // Per-subaccount Tavily usage logging for billing
2868:    logSearchUsage(context.subaccountId, context.organisationId, context.runId).catch((err) => console.error('[SkillExecutor] Failed to log search usage:', err));
2869:
2870:    return {
2871:      success: true,
2872:      answer: data.answer ?? null,
2873:      results: (data.results ?? []).map(r => ({
2874:        title: r.title,
2875:        url: r.url,
2876:        content: r.content,
2877:        relevance_score: r.score,
2878:      })),
2879:    };
2880:  } catch (err) {
2881:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
2882:    return { success: false, error: `Search failed: ${errMsg}` };
2883:  }
2884:}
2885:
2886:function logSearchUsage(subaccountId: string | null, organisationId: string, runId: string): Promise<void> {
2887:  // Structured usage log for per-subaccount Tavily billing tracking.
2888:  // Log aggregation (e.g. Datadog, CloudWatch) captures this for billing.
2889:  console.log(JSON.stringify({
2890:    event: 'platform_usage',
2891:    service: 'tavily_search',
2892:    calls: 1,
2893:    subaccountId,
2894:    organisationId,
2895:    runId,
2896:    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
2897:  }));
2898:  return Promise.resolve();
2899:}
