2901:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2902:// Read Workspace
2903:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2904:
2905:async function executeReadWorkspace(
2906:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
2907:  context: SkillExecutionContext
2908:): Promise<unknown> {
2909:  const limit = Math.min(Number(input.limit ?? 20), 50);
2910:  const includeActivities = Boolean(input.include_activities);
2911:
2912:  try {
2913:    // Single-task lookup by ID
2914:    if (input.task_id) {
2915:      const task = await taskService.getTask(String(input.task_id), context.organisationId);
2916:      return { success: true, item: serializeTask(task), total: 1 };
2917:    }
2918:
2919:    // Subtask listing by parent
2920:    if (input.parent_task_id) {
2921:      const parentId = String(input.parent_task_id);
2922:      const allItems = await taskService.listTasks(context.organisationId, context.subaccountId!, {});
2923:      const subtasks = allItems.filter(t => (t as { parentTaskId?: string | null }).parentTaskId === parentId);
2924:      return {
2925:        success: true,
2926:        items: subtasks.map(serializeTask),
2927:        total: subtasks.length,
2928:        allDone: subtasks.length > 0 && subtasks.every(t => t.status === 'done'),
2929:        // Task status enum (server/db/schema/tasks.ts) has no 'blocked' value today;
2930:        // field reserved for a future status. Always false at runtime under the current schema.
2931:        anyBlocked: false,
2932:      };
2933:    }
2934:
2935:    // Standard filtered listing
2936:    const filters: { status?: string; assignedAgentId?: string } = {};
2937:    if (input.status) filters.status = String(input.status);
2938:    if (input.assigned_to_me) filters.assignedAgentId = context.agentId;
2939:
2940:    const items = await taskService.listTasks(context.organisationId, context.subaccountId!, filters);
2941:    const sliced = items.slice(0, limit);
2942:
2943:    if (includeActivities) {
2944:      const enriched = await Promise.all(sliced.map(async (item) => {
2945:        const activities = await taskService.listActivities(item.id, context.organisationId);
2946:        return {
2947:          ...serializeTask(item),
2948:          activities: activities.slice(0, 5).map(a => ({
2949:            type: a.activityType,
2950:            message: a.message,
2951:            createdAt: a.createdAt,
2952:          })),
2953:        };
2954:      }));
2955:      return { success: true, items: enriched, total: items.length };
2956:    }
2957:
2958:    return { success: true, items: sliced.map(serializeTask), total: items.length };
2959:  } catch (err) {
2960:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
2961:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to read board: ${errMsg}` };
2962:  }
2963:}
2964:
2965:function serializeTask(item: Record<string, unknown>): Record<string, unknown> {
2966:  return {
2967:    id: item.id,
2968:    title: item.title,
2969:    description: item.description,
2970:    brief: item.brief,
2971:    status: item.status,
2972:    priority: item.priority,
2973:    isSubTask: (item as { isSubTask?: boolean }).isSubTask ?? false,
2974:    parentTaskId: (item as { parentTaskId?: string | null }).parentTaskId ?? null,
2975:    assignedAgent: item.assignedAgent,
2976:    createdAt: item.createdAt,
2977:  };
2978:}

2984:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2985:// write_spec ŌĆö post-approval executor
2986:// Writes the approved spec to workspace memory and marks the task spec-approved.
2987:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
2988:
2989:async function executeWriteSpecApproved(
2990:  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
2991:  context: SkillExecutionContext
2992:): Promise<unknown> {
2993:  const taskId = String(payload.task_id ?? '');
2994:  const specContent = String(payload.spec_content ?? '');
2995:  const reasoning = String(payload.reasoning ?? '');
2996:  const storiesCount = Number(payload.user_stories_count ?? 0);
2997:  const acCount = Number(payload.ac_count ?? 0);
2998:
2999:  if (!taskId) return { success: false, error: 'task_id is required' };
3000:  if (!specContent) return { success: false, error: 'spec_content is required' };
3001:
3002:  // Build a stable spec reference ID so QA / Dev can retrieve this spec by key.
3003:  // Pattern: SPEC-<taskId>-v<N> ŌĆö we derive N from activity count to ensure
3004:  // monotonically increasing version without a dedicated DB column.
3005:  let version = 1;
3006:  try {
3007:    const existing = await taskService.listActivities(taskId, context.organisationId);
3008:    const priorSpecs = existing.filter((a: { activityType: string; message: string }) =>
3009:      a.activityType === 'note' && a.message.startsWith('SPEC_APPROVED:')
3010:    );
3011:    version = priorSpecs.length + 1;
3012:  } catch { /* treat as first version */ }
3013:
3014:  const specReferenceId = `SPEC-${taskId}-v${version}`;
3015:
3016:  try {
3017:    // 1. Write the spec to workspace memory as a structured activity.
3018:    await taskService.addActivity(taskId, context.organisationId, {
3019:      activityType: 'note',
3020:      message: `SPEC_APPROVED:${specReferenceId}\n\n${specContent}`,
3021:      agentId: context.agentId,
3022:    });
3023:
3024:    // 2. Write a human-readable summary activity for the board.
3025:    await taskService.addActivity(taskId, context.organisationId, {
3026:      activityType: 'completed',
3027:      message: `Requirements spec approved.\nReference: ${specReferenceId}\nStories: ${storiesCount} | ACs: ${acCount}\nReasoning: ${reasoning}`,
3028:      agentId: context.agentId,
3029:    });
3030:
3031:    // 3. Advance task status to spec-approved.
3032:    await taskService.updateTask(taskId, context.organisationId, { status: 'spec-approved' });
3033:
3034:    return {
3035:      success: true,
3036:      spec_reference_id: specReferenceId,
3037:      task_id: taskId,
3038:      message: `Spec ${specReferenceId} approved and written to workspace memory. Task status updated to spec-approved.`,
3039:    };
3040:  } catch (err) {
3041:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3042:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to persist approved spec: ${errMsg}` };
3043:  }
3044:}

3052:async function executePublishPostApproved(
3053:  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
3054:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3055:): Promise<unknown> {
3056:  const platform = String(payload.platform ?? '');
3057:  const postContent = String(payload.post_content ?? '');
3058:  const scheduleAt = payload.schedule_at ? String(payload.schedule_at) : null;
3059:  const campaignTag = payload.campaign_tag ? String(payload.campaign_tag) : null;
3060:  const reasoning = String(payload.reasoning ?? '');
3061:
3062:  if (!platform) return { success: false, error: 'platform is required' };
3063:  if (!postContent) return { success: false, error: 'post_content is required' };
3064:
3065:  // Log publish action to workspace memory if a taskId is available
3066:  if (context.taskId) {
3067:    try {
3068:      const logMsg = [
3069:        `PUBLISH_POST_APPROVED:${platform}`,
3070:        `campaign: ${campaignTag ?? 'none'}`,
3071:        scheduleAt ? `scheduled: ${scheduleAt}` : 'publish: immediate',
3072:        `reasoning: ${reasoning}`,
3073:        `---\n${postContent}`,
3074:      ].join('\n');
3075:
3076:      await taskService.addActivity(context.taskId, context.organisationId, {
3077:        activityType: 'note',
3078:        message: logMsg,
3079:        agentId: context.agentId,
3080:      });
3081:    } catch { /* non-fatal ŌĆö log failure does not block publish response */ }
3082:  }
3083:
3084:  return {
3085:    success: true,
3086:    platform,
3087:    publish_status: 'pending_integration',
3088:    scheduled_for: scheduleAt,
3089:    campaign_tag: campaignTag,
3090:    message: `Publish approved for ${platform}. Platform integration not yet connected ŌĆö action logged. When integration is live, this will ${scheduleAt ? `schedule the post for ${scheduleAt}` : 'publish immediately'}.`,
3091:  };
3092:}

3305:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3306:// executeConfigureIntegrationApproved ŌĆö MVP stub for configure_integration.
3307:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3308:
3309:/** Redact fields whose keys match common credential patterns before storage. */
3310:const SENSITIVE_KEY_PATTERN = /(^|_)(key|secret|token|password|credential|auth|bearer)|api_key|client_secret|access_token|refresh_token/i;
3311:
3312:function redactSensitiveFields(obj: Record<string, unknown>): Record<string, unknown> {
3313:  const result: Record<string, unknown> = {};
3314:  for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(obj)) {
3315:    if (SENSITIVE_KEY_PATTERN.test(key)) {
3316:      result[key] = '[REDACTED]';
3317:    } else if (value && typeof value === 'object' && !Array.isArray(value)) {
3318:      result[key] = redactSensitiveFields(value as Record<string, unknown>);
3319:    } else {
3320:      result[key] = value;
3321:    }
3322:  }
3323:  return result;
3324:}
3325:
3326:async function executeConfigureIntegrationApproved(
3327:  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
3328:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3329:): Promise<unknown> {
3330:  const integrationType = String(payload.integration_type ?? '');
3331:  const providerName = String(payload.provider_name ?? '');
3332:  const reasoning = String(payload.reasoning ?? '');
3333:  const configuration = (payload.configuration as Record<string, unknown>) ?? {};
3334:
3335:  if (!integrationType) return { success: false, error: 'integration_type is required' };
3336:  if (!providerName) return { success: false, error: 'provider_name is required' };
3337:
3338:  // Redact sensitive fields before any storage
3339:  const redactedConfig = redactSensitiveFields(configuration);
3340:
3341:  if (context.taskId) {
3342:    try {
3343:      await taskService.addActivity(context.taskId, context.organisationId, {
3344:        activityType: 'note',
3345:        message: `INTEGRATION_APPROVED:${integrationType}:${providerName}\nreasoning: ${reasoning}\nconfig: ${JSON.stringify(redactedConfig)}`,
3346:        agentId: context.agentId,
3347:      });
3348:    } catch { /* non-fatal */ }
3349:  }
3350:
3351:  return {
3352:    success: true,
3353:    integration_type: integrationType,
3354:    provider_name: providerName,
3355:    configuration: redactedConfig,
3356:    status: 'pending_integration',
3357:    message: `Integration configuration approved (${integrationType}: ${providerName}). Integration storage not yet connected ŌĆö configuration logged with credentials redacted.`,
3358:  };
3359:}

3366:async function executeDocProposalApproved(
3367:  payload: Record<string, unknown>,
3368:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3369:): Promise<unknown> {
3370:  const pageTitle = String(payload.page_title ?? '');
3371:  const changeType = String(payload.change_type ?? '');
3372:  const changesCount = Array.isArray(payload.proposed_changes) ? payload.proposed_changes.length : 0;
3373:
3374:  if (context.taskId) {
3375:    try {
3376:      await taskService.addActivity(context.taskId, context.organisationId, {
3377:        activityType: 'note',
3378:        message: `DOC_PROPOSAL_APPROVED:${pageTitle}\nchange_type: ${changeType}\nchanges: ${changesCount}`,
3379:        agentId: context.agentId,
3380:      });
3381:    } catch { /* non-fatal */ }
3382:  }
3383:
3384:  return {
3385:    success: true,
3386:    page_title: pageTitle,
3387:    changes_approved: changesCount,
3388:    message: `Doc update proposal approved for "${pageTitle}". Invoke write_docs with the full updated content to apply the changes.`,
3389:  };
3390:}

3397:  payload: Record<string, unknown>,

3402:  const reasoning = String(payload.reasoning ?? '');

3404:  if (!pageTitle) return { success: false, error: 'page_title is required' };

3406:  if (context.taskId) {

3427:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
3428:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3429:): Promise<unknown> {

3432:  const message = String(input.message ?? '');
3433:

3435:  if (!message) return { success: false, error: 'message is required' };

3439:      activityType,
3440:      message,

3442:    });
3443:
3444:    return { success: true, activity_id: activity.id, _updated_task: true };
3445:  } catch (err) {
3446:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3447:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to write to board: ${errMsg}` };
3448:  }

3452:// Trigger Task
3453:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3454:
3455:async function executeTriggerProcess(
3456:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
3457:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3458:): Promise<unknown> {
3459:  const processId = String(input.process_id ?? '');
3460:  const inputData = String(input.input_data ?? '{}');
3461:  const reason = String(input.reason ?? '');
3462:  const configOverridesStr = String(input.config_overrides ?? '{}');
3463:
3464:  if (!processId) return { success: false, error: 'process_id is required' };
3465:
3466:  let configOverrides: Record<string, unknown> | undefined;
3467:  try {
3468:    const parsed = JSON.parse(configOverridesStr);
3469:    if (parsed && typeof parsed === 'object' && Object.keys(parsed).length > 0) {
3470:      configOverrides = parsed;
3471:    }
3472:  } catch { /* ignore parse errors */ }
3473:
3474:  try {
3475:    const result = await executeTriggerredProcess(
3476:      context.organisationId,
3477:      processId,
3478:      context.agentId,
3479:      inputData,
3480:      {
3481:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? undefined,
3482:        triggerType: 'agent',
3483:        triggerSourceId: context.runId,
3484:        configOverrides,
3485:      }
3486:    );
3487:
3488:    return {
3489:      success: true,
3490:      execution_id: result.executionId,
3491:      process_name: result.processName,
3492:      status: result.status,
3493:      message: `Process "${result.processName}" has been queued. Execution ID: ${result.executionId}`,
3494:    };
3495:  } catch (err) {
3496:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3497:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to trigger process: ${errMsg}` };
3498:  }
3499:}
3500:
3501:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3502:// Create Task ŌĆö with handoff support
3503:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3504:
3505:async function executeCreateTask(
3506:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
3507:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3508:): Promise<unknown> {
3509:  const title = String(input.title ?? '').slice(0, MAX_TASK_TITLE_LENGTH);
3510:  if (!title) return { success: false, error: 'title is required' };
3511:
3512:  // Support both singular assigned_agent_id and plural assigned_agent_ids array
3513:  const rawSingular = input.assigned_agent_id ? String(input.assigned_agent_id) : undefined;
3514:  const rawPlural = Array.isArray(input.assigned_agent_ids)
3515:    ? (input.assigned_agent_ids as unknown[]).map(String)
3516:    : rawSingular ? [rawSingular] : [];
3517:  const assignedAgentIds = [...new Set(rawPlural.filter(Boolean))];
3518:
3519:  // Self-assignment prevention
3520:  if (assignedAgentIds.includes(context.agentId)) {
3521:    return { success: false, error: 'Cannot assign a task to yourself ŌĆö this would create an infinite loop. Assign to a different agent or leave unassigned.' };
3522:  }
3523:
3524:  // Validate priority
3525:  const rawPriority = String(input.priority ?? 'normal');
3526:  const priority: TaskPriority = (VALID_PRIORITIES as readonly string[]).includes(rawPriority)
3527:    ? rawPriority as TaskPriority
3528:    : 'normal';
3529:
3530:  const description = input.description ? String(input.description).slice(0, MAX_TASK_DESCRIPTION_LENGTH) : undefined;
3531:  const handoffContext = input.handoff_context ? String(input.handoff_context) : undefined;
3532:  const currentDepth = context.handoffDepth ?? 0;
3533:
3534:  // Check handoff depth BEFORE creating the task to avoid orphans
3535:  if (assignedAgentIds.length > 0 && currentDepth + 1 > MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH) {
3536:    return {
3537:      success: false,
3538:      error: `Handoff depth limit (${MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH}) reached. Cannot assign task to another agent at this depth. Create the task without assignment instead.`,
3539:    };
3540:  }
3541:
3542:  try {
3543:    const tx = getOrgScopedDb('service:skillExecutor.executeCreateTask');
3544:    const item = await taskService.createTask(
3545:      {
3546:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
3547:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
3548:        data: {
3549:          title,
3550:          description,
3551:          brief: input.brief ? String(input.brief) : undefined,
3552:          priority,
3553:          status: input.status ? String(input.status) : 'inbox',
3554:          assignedAgentIds: assignedAgentIds.length ? assignedAgentIds : undefined,
3555:          createdByAgentId: context.agentId,
3556:          handoffSourceRunId: context.runId,
3557:          handoffContext: handoffContext ? { message: handoffContext } : undefined,
3558:          handoffDepth: assignedAgentIds.length ? currentDepth + 1 : 0,
3559:        },
3560:      },
3561:      tx,
3562:    );
3563:
3564:    // Trigger a handoff for every assigned agent
3565:    const handoffResults = await Promise.all(
3566:      assignedAgentIds.map(agentId =>
3567:        enqueueHandoff({
3568:          taskId: item.id,
3569:          agentId,
3570:          subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
3571:          organisationId: context.organisationId,
3572:          sourceRunId: context.runId,
3573:          handoffDepth: currentDepth + 1,
3574:          handoffContext,
3575:        })
3576:      )
3577:    );
3578:    const handoffsEnqueued = handoffResults.filter(Boolean).length;
3579:
3580:    return {
3581:      success: true,
3582:      task_id: item.id,
3583:      title: item.title,
3584:      status: item.status,
3585:      assigned_agent_ids: assignedAgentIds,
3586:      handoffs_enqueued: handoffsEnqueued,
3587:      _created_task: true,
3588:    };
3589:  } catch (err) {
3590:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3591:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to create task: ${errMsg}` };
3592:  }
3593:}
3594:
3595:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3596:// Triage Intake ŌĆö capture and route ideas/bugs into the inbox
3597://
3598:// Two modes:
3599://   - capture: fast, judgement-free intake of one item. Builds a structured
3600://              description and creates a task in the 'inbox' status column.
3601://              Bugs that mention data corruption/data loss are auto-escalated
3602://              to priority='urgent'.
3603://   - triage:  scans the inbox for tasks lacking a triage disposition and
3604://              returns a structured proposal list (type_inferred, suggested
3605://              disposition, rationale). The skill is a *proposer*, not an
3606://              applier ŌĆö the caller (orchestrator or human) decides which
3607://              dispositions to apply via move_task / update_task.
3608://
3609:// Spec: server/skills/triage_intake.md
3610:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3611:
3612:const DATA_LOSS_PATTERN =
3613:  /\b(data\s*loss|data\s*corruption|corrupted|lost\s+data|wrong\s+data\s+written|cannot\s+recover|deleted\s+(?:rows?|records?)|overwritten|stale\s+writes?)\b/i;
3614:
3615:const TRIAGE_DECISION_MARKER = 'Triage decision:';
3616:
3617:function buildIdeaDescription(args: {
3618:  source: string;
3619:  rawInput: string;
3620:  relatedTaskId?: string;
3621:}): string {
3622:  return [
3623:    `Task type: idea`,
3624:    `Origin: ${args.source}`,
3625:    `Related task: ${args.relatedTaskId ?? 'None'}`,
3626:    ``,
3627:    `Problem / Opportunity:`,
3628:    args.rawInput.trim(),
3629:    ``,
3630:    `Notes:`,
3631:    `Captured via triage_intake (capture mode). Awaiting triage disposition ŌĆö the orchestrator or a human will assess scope, value, and routing in the next triage pass.`,
3632:  ].join('\n');
3633:}
3634:
3635:function buildBugDescription(args: {
3636:  source: string;
3637:  rawInput: string;
3638:  relatedTaskId?: string;
3639:  dataLossEscalated: boolean;
3640:}): string {
3641:  return [
3642:    `Task type: bug`,
3643:    `Origin: ${args.source}`,
3644:    `Related task: ${args.relatedTaskId ?? 'None'}`,
3645:    ``,
3646:    `Reported behaviour:`,
3647:    args.rawInput.trim(),
3648:    ``,
3649:    `Expected behaviour:`,
3650:    `(to be filled in during triage)`,
3651:    ``,
3652:    `Reproduction steps:`,
3653:    `(to be filled in during triage)`,
3654:    ``,
3655:    `Impact estimate:`,
3656:    `- Users affected: Unknown`,
3657:    `- Data impact: ${args.dataLossEscalated ? 'POSSIBLE DATA LOSS ŌĆö escalated to urgent priority' : 'Unknown'}`,
3658:    `- Workaround exists: Unknown`,
3659:    args.dataLossEscalated
3660:      ? `\nŌÜĀ AUTO-ESCALATED: data-loss/corruption keywords detected in raw input. Priority set to urgent. Human review required before fix work begins.`
3661:      : '',
3662:  ]
3663:    .filter(Boolean)
3664:    .join('\n');
3665:}
3666:
3667:function buildChoreDescription(args: {
3668:  source: string;
3669:  rawInput: string;
3670:  relatedTaskId?: string;
3671:}): string {
3672:  return [
3673:    `Task type: chore`,
3674:    `Origin: ${args.source}`,
3675:    `Related task: ${args.relatedTaskId ?? 'None'}`,
3676:    ``,
3677:    `Description:`,
3678:    args.rawInput.trim(),
3679:    ``,
3680:    `Notes:`,
3681:    `Captured via triage_intake (capture mode). Awaiting scheduling decision.`,
3682:  ].join('\n');
3683:}
3684:
3685:function inferTypeFromDescription(description: string | null): 'idea' | 'bug' | 'chore' | 'unknown' {
3686:  if (!description) return 'unknown';
3687:  const match = description.match(/^Task type:\s*(idea|bug|chore)/im);
3688:  return (match?.[1]?.toLowerCase() as 'idea' | 'bug' | 'chore' | undefined) ?? 'unknown';
3689:}
3690:
3691:function suggestDisposition(args: {
3692:  type: ReturnType<typeof inferTypeFromDescription>;
3693:  priority: string;
3694:  description: string | null;
3695:  title: string;
3696:}): { disposition: 'Defer' | 'Assess' | 'Schedule' | 'Close'; rationale: string } {
3697:  // Urgent items always get Schedule (they need to be acted on, not deferred)
3698:  if (args.priority === 'urgent') {
3699:    return {
3700:      disposition: 'Schedule',
3701:      rationale: 'Urgent priority ŌĆö requires immediate scheduling, not deferral.',
3702:    };
3703:  }
3704:
3705:  // Bugs with data-loss markers ŌĆö already escalated above. Ordinary bugs ŌåÆ Schedule.
3706:  if (args.type === 'bug') {
3707:    return {
3708:      disposition: 'Schedule',
3709:      rationale: 'Bug reports default to schedule for fix work ŌĆö defer only after explicit assessment.',
3710:    };
3711:  }
3712:
3713:  // Chores ŌåÆ Schedule (small, predictable work)
3714:  if (args.type === 'chore') {
3715:    return {
3716:      disposition: 'Schedule',
3717:      rationale: 'Chore tasks are small and predictable ŌĆö schedule directly without spec work.',
3718:    };
3719:  }
3720:
3721:  // Ideas ŌåÆ Assess (need BA evaluation before sizing)
3722:  if (args.type === 'idea') {
3723:    return {
3724:      disposition: 'Assess',
3725:      rationale: 'Idea/feature request ŌĆö route to Business Analyst for scope and value assessment before scheduling.',
3726:    };
3727:  }
3728:
3729:  // Unknown type ŌĆö default to Defer (safer than guessing)
3730:  return {
3731:    disposition: 'Defer',
3732:    rationale: 'Unknown task type ŌĆö defer until reclassified or human reviews.',
3733:  };
3734:}
3735:
3736:async function executeTriageIntake(
3737:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
3738:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3739:): Promise<unknown> {
3740:  const mode = String(input.mode ?? '');
3741:  if (mode !== 'capture' && mode !== 'triage') {
3742:    return { success: false, error: "mode must be 'capture' or 'triage'" };
3743:  }
3744:
3745:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ CAPTURE MODE ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
3746:  if (mode === 'capture') {
3747:    const rawInput = String(input.raw_input ?? '').trim();
3748:    const inputType = String(input.input_type ?? '').toLowerCase();
3749:    const source = String(input.source ?? '').trim();
3750:    const relatedTaskId = input.related_task_id ? String(input.related_task_id) : undefined;
3751:
3752:    if (!rawInput) {
3753:      return { success: false, error: "'raw_input' is required in capture mode" };
3754:    }
3755:    if (inputType !== 'idea' && inputType !== 'bug' && inputType !== 'chore') {
3756:      return {
3757:        success: false,
3758:        error: "'input_type' must be one of: idea, bug, chore",
3759:      };
3760:    }
3761:    if (!source) {
3762:      return { success: false, error: "'source' is required in capture mode" };
3763:    }
3764:
3765:    // Detect data-loss escalation for bugs (per spec escalation rule)
3766:    const dataLossEscalated = inputType === 'bug' && DATA_LOSS_PATTERN.test(rawInput);
3767:
3768:    // Map intake type ŌåÆ runtime priority. Bugs with data-loss markers escalate
3769:    // to 'urgent'; everything else defaults to 'normal'. Triage mode is the
3770:    // place where priorities get adjusted further if needed.
3771:    const priority: TaskPriority = dataLossEscalated ? 'urgent' : 'normal';
3772:
3773:    // Build the structured description per the spec template
3774:    let description: string;
3775:    if (inputType === 'idea') {
3776:      description = buildIdeaDescription({ source, rawInput, relatedTaskId });
3777:    } else if (inputType === 'bug') {
3778:      description = buildBugDescription({ source, rawInput, relatedTaskId, dataLossEscalated });
3779:    } else {
3780:      description = buildChoreDescription({ source, rawInput, relatedTaskId });
3781:    }
3782:
3783:    // Title: first line of raw input, truncated. Capture mode is allowed to
3784:    // be lossy here ŌĆö the structured description carries the full content.
3785:    const title = rawInput.split(/\n/, 1)[0]!.slice(0, MAX_TASK_TITLE_LENGTH).trim() || `${inputType} from ${source}`;
3786:
3787:    try {
3788:      const tx = getOrgScopedDb('service:skillExecutor.executeTriageIntake');
3789:      const item = await taskService.createTask(
3790:        {
3791:          organisationId: context.organisationId,
3792:          subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
3793:          data: {
3794:            title,
3795:            description: description.slice(0, MAX_TASK_DESCRIPTION_LENGTH),
3796:            priority,
3797:            status: 'inbox',
3798:            createdByAgentId: context.agentId,
3799:          },
3800:        },
3801:        tx,
3802:      );
3803:
3804:      return {
3805:        success: true,
3806:        mode: 'capture' as const,
3807:        task_id: item.id,
3808:        title: item.title,
3809:        captured_type: inputType,
3810:        priority,
3811:        escalated: dataLossEscalated,
3812:        _created_task: true,
3813:      };
3814:    } catch (err) {
3815:      const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3816:      return { success: false, error: `Failed to capture task: ${errMsg}` };
3817:    }
3818:  }
3819:
3820:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ TRIAGE MODE ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
3821:  // Scan the inbox for items lacking a triage disposition and return a
3822:  // structured proposal list. This skill does NOT apply dispositions ŌĆö
3823:  // the caller (orchestrator or human) does that via move_task/update_task.
3824:  const scope = String(input.scope ?? 'all');
3825:  const relatedTaskId = input.related_task_id ? String(input.related_task_id) : undefined;
3826:
3827:  if (scope === 'single' && !relatedTaskId) {
3828:    return { success: false, error: "'related_task_id' is required when scope='single'" };
3829:  }
3830:
3831:  try {
3832:    const conditions = [
3833:      eq(tasks.subaccountId, context.subaccountId!),
3834:      eq(tasks.status, 'inbox'),
3835:      isActive(tasks),
3836:    ];
3837:    if (scope === 'single' && relatedTaskId) {
3838:      conditions.push(eq(tasks.id, relatedTaskId));
3839:    }
3840:
3841:    const inboxRows = await db
3842:      .select({
3843:        id: tasks.id,
3844:        title: tasks.title,
3845:        description: tasks.description,
3846:        priority: tasks.priority,
3847:        createdAt: tasks.createdAt,
3848:      })
3849:      .from(tasks)
3850:      .where(and(...conditions));
3851:
3852:    // Filter out items that already carry a triage decision marker ŌĆö those
3853:    // have been triaged in a previous pass and are awaiting application.
3854:    const untriaged = inboxRows.filter(
3855:      (row) => !row.description?.includes(TRIAGE_DECISION_MARKER)
3856:    );
3857:
3858:    const proposals = untriaged.map((row) => {
3859:      const type = inferTypeFromDescription(row.description);
3860:      const { disposition, rationale } = suggestDisposition({
3861:        type,
3862:        priority: row.priority,
3863:        description: row.description,
3864:        title: row.title,
3865:      });
3866:      return {
3867:        task_id: row.id,
3868:        title: row.title,
3869:        type_inferred: type,
3870:        priority: row.priority,
3871:        suggested_disposition: disposition,
3872:        rationale,
3873:      };
3874:    });
3875:
3876:    // Group counts for the summary block
3877:    const byDisposition = proposals.reduce<Record<string, number>>((acc, p) => {
3878:      acc[p.suggested_disposition] = (acc[p.suggested_disposition] ?? 0) + 1;
3879:      return acc;
3880:    }, {});
3881:
3882:    return {
3883:      success: true,
3884:      mode: 'triage' as const,
3885:      scope,
3886:      scanned: inboxRows.length,
3887:      already_triaged: inboxRows.length - untriaged.length,
3888:      proposals_returned: proposals.length,
3889:      summary: byDisposition,
3890:      proposals,
3891:    };
3892:  } catch (err) {
3893:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3894:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to scan inbox for triage: ${errMsg}` };
3895:  }
3896:}
3897:
3898:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3899:// Move Task
3900:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3901:
3902:async function executeMoveTask(
3903:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
3904:  context: SkillExecutionContext
3905:): Promise<unknown> {
3906:  const taskId = String(input.task_id ?? '');
3907:  const status = String(input.status ?? '');
3908:
3909:  if (!taskId) return { success: false, error: 'task_id is required' };
3910:  if (!status) return { success: false, error: 'status is required' };
3911:
3912:  try {
3913:    // Get current item to find subaccount
3914:    const item = await taskService.getTask(taskId, context.organisationId);
3915:    const position = await taskService._nextPosition(item.subaccountId!, status as Parameters<typeof taskService._nextPosition>[1]);
3916:
3917:    const updated = await taskService.moveTask(
3918:      taskId,
3919:      context.organisationId,
3920:      { status, position }
3921:    );
3922:
3923:    return {
3924:      success: true,
3925:      task_id: updated.id,
3926:      new_status: updated.status,
3927:      _updated_task: true,
3928:    };
3929:  } catch (err) {
3930:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
3931:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to move task: ${errMsg}` };
3932:  }
3933:}

3976:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3977:// Handoff enqueuing
3978:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
3979:
3980:interface HandoffRequest {
3981:  taskId: string;
3982:  agentId: string;
3983:  subaccountId: string;
3984:  organisationId: string;
3985:  sourceRunId: string;
3986:  handoffDepth: number;
3987:  handoffContext?: string;
3988:}
3989:
3990:async function enqueueHandoff(req: HandoffRequest): Promise<boolean> {
3991:  // Depth cap
3992:  if (req.handoffDepth > MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH) {
3993:    console.warn(`[Handoff] Depth ${req.handoffDepth} exceeds max ${MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH}, skipping`);
3994:    return false;
3995:  }
3996:
3997:  // Look up the subaccount agent link for the target agent
3998:  const [saLink] = await db
3999:    .select({
4000:      sa: subaccountAgents,
4001:    })
4002:    .from(subaccountAgents)
4003:    .innerJoin(agents, and(eq(agents.id, subaccountAgents.agentId), isActive(agents)))
4004:    .where(
4005:      and(
4006:        eq(subaccountAgents.subaccountId, req.subaccountId),
4007:        eq(subaccountAgents.agentId, req.agentId),
4008:        eq(subaccountAgents.isActive, true),
4009:        eq(agents.status, 'active'),
4010:      )
4011:    );
4012:
4013:  if (!saLink) {
4014:    console.warn(`[Handoff] No active subaccount agent link for agent ${req.agentId} in subaccount ${req.subaccountId}`);
4015:    return false;
4016:  }
4017:
4018:  // Duplicate prevention: check for running/pending runs for same agent+task
4019:  const [existingRun] = await db
4020:    .select()
4021:    .from(agentRuns)
4022:    .where(
4023:      and(
4024:        eq(agentRuns.agentId, req.agentId),
4025:        eq(agentRuns.taskId, req.taskId),
4026:        eq(agentRuns.subaccountId, req.subaccountId)
4027:      )
4028:    )
4029:    .limit(1);
4030:
4031:  if (existingRun && (existingRun.status === 'running' || existingRun.status === 'pending')) {
4032:    console.warn(`[Handoff] Agent ${req.agentId} already has a ${existingRun.status} run for task ${req.taskId}, skipping`);
4033:    return false;
4034:  }
4035:
4036:  if (!pgBossSend) {
4037:    console.warn('[Handoff] pg-boss sender not configured, cannot enqueue handoff');
4038:    return false;
4039:  }
4040:
4041:  try {
4042:    await pgBossSend(AGENT_HANDOFF_QUEUE, {
4043:      taskId: req.taskId,
4044:      agentId: req.agentId,
4045:      subaccountAgentId: saLink.sa.id,
4046:      subaccountId: req.subaccountId,
4047:      organisationId: req.organisationId,
4048:      sourceRunId: req.sourceRunId,
4049:      handoffDepth: req.handoffDepth,
4050:      handoffContext: req.handoffContext,
4051:    });
4052:    createEvent('agent.handoff.enqueued', {
4053:      targetAgentId: req.agentId,
4054:      sourceRunId: req.sourceRunId,
4055:      handoffDepth: req.handoffDepth,
4056:      taskId: req.taskId,
4057:    });
4058:    return true;
4059:  } catch (err) {
4060:    console.error('[Handoff] Failed to enqueue handoff job:', err);
4061:    return false;
4062:  }
4063:}

4065:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4066:// Update Task ŌĆö update content fields (title, description, brief, priority)
4067:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4068:
4069:async function executeUpdateTask(
4070:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
4071:  context: SkillExecutionContext
4072:): Promise<unknown> {
4073:  const taskId = String(input.task_id ?? '');
4074:  if (!taskId) return { success: false, error: 'task_id is required' };
4075:
4076:  const reasoning = String(input.reasoning ?? '').trim();
4077:  if (!reasoning) return { success: false, error: 'reasoning is required' };
4078:
4079:  const update: {
4080:    title?: string;
4081:    description?: string;
4082:    brief?: string;
4083:    priority?: 'low' | 'normal' | 'high' | 'urgent';
4084:  } = {};
4085:
4086:  if (input.title !== undefined) update.title = String(input.title).slice(0, 255);
4087:  if (input.description !== undefined) update.description = String(input.description);
4088:  if (input.brief !== undefined) update.brief = String(input.brief);
4089:  if (input.priority !== undefined) {
4090:    const p = String(input.priority);
4091:    if (!['low', 'normal', 'high', 'urgent'].includes(p)) {
4092:      return { success: false, error: `Invalid priority: ${p}` };
4093:    }
4094:    update.priority = p as 'low' | 'normal' | 'high' | 'urgent';
4095:  }
4096:
4097:  if (!Object.keys(update).length) {
4098:    return { success: false, error: 'At least one field (title, description, brief, priority) must be provided' };
4099:  }
4100:
4101:  try {
4102:    const updated = await taskService.updateTask(taskId, context.organisationId, update);
4103:
4104:    await taskService.addActivity(taskId, context.organisationId, {
4105:      activityType: 'note',
4106:      message: `Updated by agent: ${reasoning}`,
4107:      agentId: context.agentId,
4108:    });
4109:
4110:    return {
4111:      success: true,
4112:      task_id: updated.id,
4113:      updated_fields: Object.keys(update),
4114:      _updated_task: true,
4115:    };
4116:  } catch (err) {
4117:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
4118:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to update task: ${errMsg}` };
4119:  }
4120:}

4122:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4123:// Reassign Task ŌĆö hand current task to another agent
4124:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4125:
4126:async function executeReassignTask(
4127:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
4128:  context: SkillExecutionContext
4129:): Promise<unknown> {
4130:  // --- STEP 1: Evaluate preconditions (hierarchy context) ---
4131:  const reassignPre = evaluateReassignPreconditions({ hierarchy: context.hierarchy });
4132:  if (!reassignPre.ok) {
4133:    const errorCtx = {
4134:      runId: context.runId,
4135:      callerAgentId: context.agentId,
4136:      skillSlug: 'reassign_task',
4137:    };
4138:    void insertExecutionEventSafe({
4139:      runId: context.runId,
4140:      organisationId: context.organisationId,
4141:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4142:      payload: { eventType: 'tool.error', critical: false, error: { code: HIERARCHY_CONTEXT_MISSING, message: 'Hierarchy context is missing', context: errorCtx } },
4143:      sourceService: 'skillExecutor',
4144:    });
4145:    return { success: false, error: HIERARCHY_CONTEXT_MISSING, context: errorCtx };
4146:  }
4147:
4148:  const hierarchy = context.hierarchy!;
4149:
4150:  // --- STEP 2: Input parsing ---
4151:  const taskId = String(input.task_id ?? '');
4152:  const handoffContext = input.handoff_context ? String(input.handoff_context) : undefined;
4153:
4154:  if (!taskId) return { success: false, error: 'task_id is required' };
4155:
4156:  const rawSingular = input.assigned_agent_id ? String(input.assigned_agent_id) : undefined;
4157:  const rawPlural = Array.isArray(input.assigned_agent_ids)
4158:    ? (input.assigned_agent_ids as unknown[]).map(String)
4159:    : rawSingular ? [rawSingular] : [];
4160:  const assignedAgentIds = [...new Set(rawPlural.filter(Boolean))];
4161:
4162:  if (!assignedAgentIds.length) return { success: false, error: 'assigned_agent_id or assigned_agent_ids is required' };
4163:
4164:  // Self-assignment prevention
4165:  if (assignedAgentIds.includes(context.agentId)) {
4166:    return { success: false, error: 'Cannot reassign a task to yourself. Choose a different agent.' };
4167:  }
4168:
4169:  // --- STEP 3: Depth check ---
4170:  const currentDepth = context.handoffDepth ?? 0;
4171:  if (currentDepth + 1 > MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH) {
4172:    return { success: false, error: `Handoff depth limit (${MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH}) reached. Cannot reassign further.` };
4173:  }
4174:
4175:  // --- STEP 4: Compute effective scope ---
4176:  const effectiveScope = resolveWriteSkillScope({ rawScope: input.delegationScope, hierarchy });
4177:
4178:  // --- STEP 5: Resolve saLinks and validate scope for each target ---
4179:  // Load descendant ids once if needed (single round trip for all targets)
4180:  let descendantIds: string[] = [];
4181:  if (effectiveScope === 'descendants') {
4182:    const rosterRows = await db
4183:      .select({
4184:        subaccountAgentId: subaccountAgents.id,
4185:        agentId: subaccountAgents.agentId,
4186:        parentSubaccountAgentId: subaccountAgents.parentSubaccountAgentId,
4187:      })
4188:      .from(subaccountAgents)
4189:      .where(
4190:        and(
4191:          eq(subaccountAgents.subaccountId, context.subaccountId!),
4192:          eq(subaccountAgents.organisationId, context.organisationId),
4193:          eq(subaccountAgents.isActive, true)
4194:        )
4195:      );
4196:    descendantIds = computeDescendantIds({
4197:      callerSubaccountAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4198:      roster: rosterRows.map(r => ({
4199:        subaccountAgentId: r.subaccountAgentId,
4200:        agentId: r.agentId,
4201:        parentSubaccountAgentId: r.parentSubaccountAgentId ?? null,
4202:      })),
4203:    });
4204:  }
4205:
4206:  const isCallerRoot = hierarchy.rootId === hierarchy.agentId;
4207:
4208:  // Validate all targets; collect resolved saLinks + directions
4209:  const resolvedAssignees: Array<{ agentId: string; saLinkId: string; direction: 'up' | 'down' | 'lateral' }> = [];
4210:
4211:  for (const agentId of assignedAgentIds) {
4212:    // Look up the subaccount agent link for this target
4213:    const [saLinkRow] = await db
4214:      .select({ sa: subaccountAgents })
4215:      .from(subaccountAgents)
4216:      .innerJoin(agents, and(eq(agents.id, subaccountAgents.agentId), isActive(agents)))
4217:      .where(
4218:        and(
4219:          eq(subaccountAgents.subaccountId, context.subaccountId!),
4220:          eq(subaccountAgents.agentId, agentId),
4221:          eq(subaccountAgents.isActive, true),
4222:          eq(agents.status, 'active'),
4223:        )
4224:      );
4225:
4226:    if (!saLinkRow) {
4227:      return { success: false, error: `Agent ${agentId} not found or inactive in this subaccount` };
4228:    }
4229:
4230:    const targetSaId = saLinkRow.sa.id;
4231:
4232:    // Compute direction ŌĆö upward escalation check BEFORE scope validation (INV-2 ordering)
4233:    const direction = computeReassignDirection({
4234:      targetSubaccountAgentId: targetSaId,
4235:      parentId: hierarchy.parentId,
4236:      childIds: hierarchy.childIds,
4237:      descendantIds,
4238:    });
4239:
4240:    // Upward escalation always permitted ŌĆö skip scope check
4241:    if (direction === 'up') {
4242:      resolvedAssignees.push({ agentId, saLinkId: targetSaId, direction });
4243:      continue;
4244:    }
4245:
4246:    // Validate scope for non-upward targets
4247:    const scopeResult = validateReassignScope({
4248:      targetSubaccountAgentId: targetSaId,
4249:      effectiveScope,
4250:      childIds: hierarchy.childIds,
4251:      descendantIds,
4252:      isCallerRoot,
4253:    });
4254:
4255:    if (!scopeResult.valid) {
4256:      void insertOutcomeSafe({
4257:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4258:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4259:        runId: context.runId,
4260:        callerAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4261:        targetAgentId: targetSaId,
4262:        delegationScope: effectiveScope,
4263:        outcome: 'rejected',
4264:        reason: scopeResult.errorCode,
4265:        delegationDirection: direction,
4266:      });
4267:      const callerChildIds = hierarchy.childIds.slice(0, 50);
4268:      const errorCtx: Record<string, unknown> = scopeResult.errorCode === 'cross_subtree_not_permitted'
4269:        ? { runId: context.runId, callerAgentId: context.agentId, callerParentId: hierarchy.parentId, suggestedScope: hierarchy.childIds.length > 0 ? 'children' : 'descendants' }
4270:        : { runId: context.runId, callerAgentId: context.agentId, targetAgentId: agentId, delegationScope: effectiveScope, callerChildIds };
4271:      if (scopeResult.errorCode === 'delegation_out_of_scope' && hierarchy.childIds.length > 50) {
4272:        errorCtx.truncated = true;
4273:      }
4274:      void insertExecutionEventSafe({
4275:        runId: context.runId,
4276:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4277:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4278:        payload: { eventType: 'tool.error', critical: false, error: { code: scopeResult.errorCode, message: scopeResult.errorCode === 'cross_subtree_not_permitted' ? 'Cross-subtree reassignment requires the caller to be the subaccount root.' : 'Reassign target is outside delegation scope.', context: errorCtx } },
4279:        sourceService: 'skillExecutor',
4280:      });
4281:      return { success: false, error: scopeResult.errorCode, context: errorCtx };
4282:    }
4283:
4284:    resolvedAssignees.push({ agentId, saLinkId: targetSaId, direction });
4285:  }
4286:
4287:  // Determine the canonical direction to store on the task.
4288:  // For single-target (typical case), use the computed direction.
4289:  // For multi-target, use 'down' if any target is down, else use the first target's direction.
4290:  const taskDelegationDirection: 'up' | 'down' | 'lateral' =
4291:    resolvedAssignees.some(a => a.direction === 'down') ? 'down' :
4292:    resolvedAssignees.some(a => a.direction === 'up') ? 'up' :
4293:    'lateral';
4294:
4295:  // --- STEP 6: Execute handoff (critical path) ---
4296:  try {
4297:    await taskService.updateTask(taskId, context.organisationId, {
4298:      assignedAgentIds,
4299:    });
4300:
4301:    // Write delegation_direction on the task (critical path)
4302:    await db.update(tasks).set({
4303:      handoffSourceRunId: context.runId,
4304:      handoffContext: handoffContext ? { message: handoffContext } : null,
4305:      handoffDepth: currentDepth + 1,
4306:      delegationDirection: taskDelegationDirection,
4307:      updatedAt: new Date(),
4308:    // guard-ignore-next-line: org-scoped-writes reason="taskId passed through taskService.updateTask above which verifies org membership; this is a supplemental metadata update on the same task"
4309:    }).where(eq(tasks.id, taskId));
4310:
4311:    await taskService.addActivity(taskId, context.organisationId, {
4312:      activityType: 'assigned',
4313:      message: `Reassigned to ${assignedAgentIds.length} agent${assignedAgentIds.length > 1 ? 's' : ''}${handoffContext ? ` ŌĆö ${handoffContext}` : ''}`,
4314:      agentId: context.agentId,
4315:    });
4316:
4317:    // Trigger a handoff for every assigned agent
4318:    const handoffResults = await Promise.all(
4319:      resolvedAssignees.map(a =>
4320:        enqueueHandoff({
4321:          taskId,
4322:          agentId: a.agentId,
4323:          subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4324:          organisationId: context.organisationId,
4325:          sourceRunId: context.runId,
4326:          handoffDepth: currentDepth + 1,
4327:          handoffContext,
4328:        })
4329:      )
4330:    );
4331:    const handoffsEnqueued = handoffResults.filter(Boolean).length;
4332:
4333:    // Write accepted outcome rows (fire-and-forget per INV-3)
4334:    for (const a of resolvedAssignees) {
4335:      void insertOutcomeSafe({
4336:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4337:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4338:        runId: context.runId,
4339:        callerAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4340:        targetAgentId: a.saLinkId,
4341:        delegationScope: effectiveScope,
4342:        outcome: 'accepted',
4343:        reason: null,
4344:        delegationDirection: a.direction,
4345:      });
4346:    }
4347:
4348:    return {
4349:      success: true,
4350:      task_id: taskId,
4351:      assigned_agent_ids: assignedAgentIds,
4352:      handoffs_enqueued: handoffsEnqueued,
4353:      _updated_task: true,
4354:    };
4355:  } catch (err) {
4356:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
4357:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to reassign task: ${errMsg}` };
4358:  }
4359:}
4360:
4361:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4362:// Spawn Sub-Agents ŌĆö parallel execution of 2-3 sub-tasks
4363:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4364:
4365:async function executeSpawnSubAgents(
4366:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
4367:  context: SkillExecutionContext
4368:): Promise<unknown> {
4369:  // --- STEP 1: Validate input structure ---
4370:  const subTasks = input.sub_tasks as Array<{ title: string; brief: string; assigned_agent_id: string }> | undefined;
4371:
4372:  if (!subTasks || !Array.isArray(subTasks)) {
4373:    return { success: false, error: 'sub_tasks array is required' };
4374:  }
4375:  if (subTasks.length < 2 || subTasks.length > MAX_SUB_AGENTS) {
4376:    return { success: false, error: `sub_tasks must contain 2-${MAX_SUB_AGENTS} items` };
4377:  }
4378:  for (const st of subTasks) {
4379:    if (!st.title || !st.brief || !st.assigned_agent_id) {
4380:      return { success: false, error: 'Each sub-task requires title, brief, and assigned_agent_id' };
4381:    }
4382:  }
4383:
4384:  // --- STEP 2: Compute effective scope ---
4385:  const effectiveScope = context.hierarchy
4386:    ? resolveWriteSkillScope({ rawScope: input.delegationScope, hierarchy: context.hierarchy })
4387:    : 'children'; // dummy ŌĆö evaluateSpawnPreconditions rejects before using this
4388:
4389:  // --- STEP 3: Evaluate preconditions (hierarchy + depth + subaccount-scope) ---
4390:  const spawnPre = evaluateSpawnPreconditions({
4391:    hierarchy: context.hierarchy,
4392:    currentHandoffDepth: context.handoffDepth ?? 0,
4393:    maxHandoffDepth: MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH,
4394:    effectiveScope,
4395:  });
4396:
4397:  if (!spawnPre.ok) {
4398:    if (spawnPre.errorCode === 'hierarchy_context_missing') {
4399:      const errorCtx = { runId: context.runId, callerAgentId: context.agentId, skillSlug: 'spawn_sub_agents' };
4400:      void insertExecutionEventSafe({
4401:        runId: context.runId,
4402:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4403:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4404:        payload: { eventType: 'tool.error', critical: false, error: { code: HIERARCHY_CONTEXT_MISSING, message: 'Hierarchy context is missing', context: errorCtx } },
4405:        sourceService: 'skillExecutor',
4406:      });
4407:      return { success: false, error: HIERARCHY_CONTEXT_MISSING, context: errorCtx };
4408:    }
4409:    if (spawnPre.errorCode === 'max_handoff_depth_exceeded') {
4410:      return { success: false, error: `Handoff depth limit (${MAX_HANDOFF_DEPTH}) reached. Cannot spawn sub-agents at this depth.` };
4411:    }
4412:    // cross_subtree_not_permitted
4413:    const hierarchy = context.hierarchy!;
4414:    const errorCtx = {
4415:      runId: context.runId,
4416:      callerAgentId: context.agentId,
4417:      callerParentId: hierarchy.parentId,
4418:      suggestedScope: hierarchy.childIds.length > 0 ? 'children' : 'descendants',
4419:    };
4420:    for (const st of subTasks) {
4421:      void insertOutcomeSafe({
4422:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4423:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4424:        runId: context.runId,
4425:        callerAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4426:        targetAgentId: st.assigned_agent_id,
4427:        delegationScope: effectiveScope,
4428:        outcome: 'rejected',
4429:        reason: CROSS_SUBTREE_NOT_PERMITTED,
4430:        delegationDirection: 'lateral',
4431:      });
4432:    }
4433:    void insertExecutionEventSafe({
4434:      runId: context.runId,
4435:      organisationId: context.organisationId,
4436:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4437:      payload: { eventType: 'tool.error', critical: false, error: { code: CROSS_SUBTREE_NOT_PERMITTED, message: 'Cross-subtree spawn is not permitted. Use children or descendants scope.', context: errorCtx } },
4438:      sourceService: 'skillExecutor',
4439:    });
4440:    return { success: false, error: CROSS_SUBTREE_NOT_PERMITTED, context: errorCtx };
4441:  }
4442:
4443:  const hierarchy = context.hierarchy!;
4444:  const safeScope = spawnPre.effectiveScope;
4445:
4446:  // --- STEP 4: Budget check ---
4447:  const totalBudget = context.tokenBudget ?? 30000;
4448:  const elapsed = context.startTime ? Date.now() - context.startTime : 0;
4449:  const totalTimeout = context.timeoutMs ?? 300000;
4450:  const remainingTimeMs = Math.max(totalTimeout - elapsed, 30000);
4451:  const perChildBudget = Math.floor(totalBudget / subTasks.length);
4452:  const perChildTimeout = Math.floor(remainingTimeMs / SUB_AGENT_TIMEOUT_BUFFER);
4453:
4454:  if (perChildBudget < MIN_SUB_AGENT_TOKEN_BUDGET) {
4455:    return { success: false, error: `Insufficient token budget remaining for ${subTasks.length} sub-agents. Need at least ${MIN_SUB_AGENT_TOKEN_BUDGET * subTasks.length} tokens.` };
4456:  }
4457:
4458:  // --- STEP 7: Resolve saLinks for all targets ---
4459:  // Must be done before scope classification because we need subaccountAgentIds.
4460:  const resolvedTargets: Array<{ st: typeof subTasks[0]; saLink: { id: string; agentId: string } }> = [];
4461:  for (const st of subTasks) {
4462:    const [saLink] = await db
4463:      .select({ sa: subaccountAgents })
4464:      .from(subaccountAgents)
4465:      .innerJoin(agents, and(eq(agents.id, subaccountAgents.agentId), isActive(agents)))
4466:      .where(
4467:        and(
4468:          eq(subaccountAgents.subaccountId, context.subaccountId!),
4469:          eq(subaccountAgents.agentId, st.assigned_agent_id),
4470:          eq(subaccountAgents.isActive, true),
4471:          eq(agents.status, 'active'),
4472:        )
4473:      );
4474:
4475:    if (!saLink) {
4476:      return { success: false, error: `Agent ${st.assigned_agent_id} not found or inactive in this subaccount` };
4477:    }
4478:
4479:    resolvedTargets.push({ st, saLink: { id: saLink.sa.id, agentId: st.assigned_agent_id } });
4480:  }
4481:
4482:  // --- STEP 8: Compute descendant ids if needed ---
4483:  let descendantIds: string[] = [];
4484:  if (safeScope === 'descendants') {
4485:    const rosterRows = await db
4486:      .select({
4487:        subaccountAgentId: subaccountAgents.id,
4488:        agentId: subaccountAgents.agentId,
4489:        parentSubaccountAgentId: subaccountAgents.parentSubaccountAgentId,
4490:      })
4491:      .from(subaccountAgents)
4492:      .where(
4493:        and(
4494:          eq(subaccountAgents.subaccountId, context.subaccountId!),
4495:          eq(subaccountAgents.organisationId, context.organisationId),
4496:          eq(subaccountAgents.isActive, true)
4497:        )
4498:      );
4499:    descendantIds = computeDescendantIds({
4500:      callerSubaccountAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4501:      roster: rosterRows.map(r => ({
4502:        subaccountAgentId: r.subaccountAgentId,
4503:        agentId: r.agentId,
4504:        parentSubaccountAgentId: r.parentSubaccountAgentId ?? null,
4505:      })),
4506:    });
4507:  }
4508:
4509:  // --- STEP 9: Scope classification ---
4510:  const { accepted, rejected } = classifySpawnTargets({
4511:    proposedSubaccountAgentIds: resolvedTargets.map(t => t.saLink.id),
4512:    effectiveScope: safeScope,
4513:    childIds: hierarchy.childIds,
4514:    descendantIds,
4515:  });
4516:
4517:  if (rejected.length > 0) {
4518:    const rejectedTargets = resolvedTargets.filter(t => rejected.includes(t.saLink.id));
4519:    for (const t of rejectedTargets) {
4520:      void insertOutcomeSafe({
4521:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4522:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4523:        runId: context.runId,
4524:        callerAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4525:        targetAgentId: t.saLink.id,
4526:        delegationScope: safeScope,
4527:        outcome: 'rejected',
4528:        reason: DELEGATION_OUT_OF_SCOPE,
4529:        delegationDirection: 'down',
4530:      });
4531:    }
4532:    const rejectedAgentIds = rejectedTargets.map(t => t.saLink.agentId);
4533:    const callerChildIds = hierarchy.childIds.slice(0, 50);
4534:    const errorCtx: Record<string, unknown> = {
4535:      runId: context.runId,
4536:      callerAgentId: context.agentId,
4537:      targetAgentId: rejectedAgentIds[0],
4538:      delegationScope: safeScope,
4539:      callerChildIds,
4540:    };
4541:    if (hierarchy.childIds.length > 50) errorCtx.truncated = true;
4542:    void insertExecutionEventSafe({
4543:      runId: context.runId,
4544:      organisationId: context.organisationId,
4545:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4546:      payload: { eventType: 'tool.error', critical: false, error: { code: DELEGATION_OUT_OF_SCOPE, message: 'One or more spawn targets are outside delegation scope.', context: errorCtx } },
4547:      sourceService: 'skillExecutor',
4548:    });
4549:    return { success: false, error: DELEGATION_OUT_OF_SCOPE, context: errorCtx };
4550:  }
4551:
4552:  // --- STEP 10: Execute spawn ---
4553:  try {
4554:    // Create task cards for all accepted targets
4555:    const childJobs: Array<{
4556:      task: { id: string; title: string };
4557:      saLink: { id: string; agentId: string };
4558:    }> = [];
4559:
4560:    for (const t of resolvedTargets) {
4561:      const tx = getOrgScopedDb('service:skillExecutor.executeSpawnSubAgents');
4562:      const task = await taskService.createTask(
4563:        {
4564:          organisationId: context.organisationId,
4565:          subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4566:          data: {
4567:            title: t.st.title.slice(0, MAX_TASK_TITLE_LENGTH),
4568:            brief: t.st.brief.slice(0, MAX_TASK_DESCRIPTION_LENGTH),
4569:            status: 'in_progress',
4570:            assignedAgentId: t.st.assigned_agent_id,
4571:            createdByAgentId: context.agentId,
4572:            isSubTask: true,
4573:            parentTaskId: context.runId,
4574:          },
4575:        },
4576:        tx,
4577:      );
4578:      childJobs.push({ task, saLink: t.saLink });
4579:    }
4580:
4581:    // Execute all children in parallel
4582:    createEvent('agent.spawn.fanout', {
4583:      fanOutCount: childJobs.length,
4584:      perChildBudget,
4585:      perChildTimeoutMs: perChildTimeout,
4586:    });
4587:    const childResults = await Promise.all(
4588:      childJobs.map(async (job) => {
4589:        try {
4590:          const result = await agentExecutionService.executeRun({
4591:            agentId: job.saLink.agentId,
4592:            subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
4593:            subaccountAgentId: job.saLink.id,
4594:            organisationId: context.organisationId,
4595:            executionScope: 'subaccount',
4596:            runType: 'triggered',
4597:            runSource: 'sub_agent',
4598:            executionMode: 'api',
4599:            taskId: job.task.id,
4600:            triggerContext: {
4601:              type: 'sub_agent',
4602:              parentRunId: context.runId,
4603:            },
4604:            isSubAgent: true,
4605:            parentSpawnRunId: context.runId,
4606:            delegationScope: safeScope,
4607:            delegationDirection: 'down',
4608:          });
4609:
4610:          return {
4611:            title: job.task.title,
4612:            status: result.status,
4613:            summary: result.summary,
4614:            task_id: job.task.id,
4615:            agent_run_id: result.runId,
4616:            tokens_used: result.totalTokens,
4617:          };
4618:        } catch (err) {
4619:          return {
4620:            title: job.task.title,
4621:            status: 'failed' as const,
4622:            summary: null,
4623:            error: err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err),
4624:            task_id: job.task.id,
4625:            agent_run_id: null,
4626:            tokens_used: 0,
4627:          };
4628:        }
4629:      })
4630:    );
4631:
4632:    // Write accepted outcome rows (fire-and-forget per INV-3)
4633:    for (const t of resolvedTargets) {
4634:      void insertOutcomeSafe({
4635:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4636:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
4637:        runId: context.runId,
4638:        callerAgentId: hierarchy.agentId,
4639:        targetAgentId: t.saLink.id,
4640:        delegationScope: safeScope,
4641:        outcome: 'accepted',
4642:        reason: null,
4643:        delegationDirection: 'down',
4644:      });
4645:    }
4646:
4647:    const totalTokens = childResults.reduce((sum, r) => sum + (r.tokens_used ?? 0), 0);
4648:
4649:    return {
4650:      success: true,
4651:      results: childResults,
4652:      total_tokens: totalTokens,
4653:      total_duration_ms: Date.now() - (context.startTime ?? Date.now()),
4654:    };
4655:  } catch (err) {
4656:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
4657:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to spawn sub-agents: ${errMsg}` };
4658:  }
4659:}

4678:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4679:// Fetch URL ŌĆö HTTP GET/POST with response truncation
4680:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4681:
4682:async function executeFetchUrl(
4683:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
4684:  _context: SkillExecutionContext
4685:): Promise<unknown> {
4686:  const url = String(input.url ?? '');
4687:  if (!url) return { success: false, error: 'url is required' };
4688:
4689:  const method = (String(input.method ?? 'GET')).toUpperCase();
4690:  if (method !== 'GET' && method !== 'POST') {
4691:    return { success: false, error: 'method must be GET or POST' };
4692:  }
4693:
4694:  const headers: Record<string, string> = {};
4695:  if (input.headers && typeof input.headers === 'object') {
4696:    for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(input.headers as Record<string, unknown>)) {
4697:      headers[k] = String(v);
4698:    }
4699:  }
4700:
4701:  try {
4702:    const fetchOptions: RequestInit = {
4703:      method,
4704:      headers,
4705:      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(30_000),
4706:    };
4707:
4708:    if (method === 'POST' && input.body) {
4709:      fetchOptions.body = String(input.body);
4710:      if (!headers['Content-Type'] && !headers['content-type']) {
4711:        headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
4712:      }
4713:    }
4714:
4715:    const response = await fetch(url, fetchOptions);
4716:
4717:    const bodyText = await response.text();
4718:    const truncated = bodyText.length > 10000;
4719:    const content = truncated ? bodyText.slice(0, 10000) : bodyText;
4720:
4721:    return {
4722:      success: true,
4723:      status_code: response.status,
4724:      content,
4725:      truncated,
4726:      content_type: response.headers.get('content-type') ?? undefined,
4727:    };
4728:  } catch (err) {
4729:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
4730:    return { success: false, error: `Fetch failed: ${errMsg}` };
4731:  }
4732:}
4733:

4735:// Scrape URL ŌĆö tiered web scraping with automatic escalation
4736:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4737:
4738:async function executeScrapeUrl(
4739:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
4740:  context: SkillExecutionContext
4741:): Promise<unknown> {
4742:  const url = String(input.url ?? '');
4743:  if (!url) return { success: false, error: 'url is required' };
4744:
4745:  const result = await scrapingEngine.scrape({
4746:    url,
4747:    extract: input.extract ? String(input.extract) : undefined,
4748:    outputFormat: (input.output_format as 'text' | 'markdown' | 'json') ?? 'markdown',
4749:    selectors: input.css_selectors as string[] | undefined,
4750:    adaptive: true,
4751:    orgId: context.organisationId,
4752:    subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? undefined,
4753:    _mcpCallContext: context._mcpClients ? {
4754:      clients: context._mcpClients,
4755:      lazyRegistry: context._mcpLazyRegistry ?? new Map(),
4756:      runContext: {
4757:        runId: context.runId,
4758:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
4759:        agentId: context.agentId,
4760:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId,
4761:        isTestRun: context.isTestRun ?? false,
4762:        taskId: context.taskId,
4763:        mcpCallCount: context.mcpCallCount,
4764:      },
4765:    } : undefined,
4766:  });
4767:
4768:  return {
4769:    success: result.success,
4770:    content: result.content,
4771:    tier_used: result.tierUsed,
4772:    content_hash: result.contentHash,
4773:    extracted_data: result.extractedData,
4774:    url: result.url,
4775:    metadata: result.metadata,
4776:  };
4777:}
4778:
4779:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4780:// Scrape Structured ŌĆö adaptive selector extraction with LLM first-run learning
4781:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
4782:
4783:const SCRAPE_STRUCTURED_MAX_HTML_CHARS = 40_000; // ~4000 tokens of focused DOM
4784:const SCRAPE_STRUCTURED_RETURN_LIMIT = 50_000;   // max response chars returned to agent
4785:
4786:/**
4787: * Derive a deterministic selectorGroup from the site hostname and field string.
4788: * Format: "<hostname>:<sha256(fields.trim().lower).slice(0,8)>"
4789: */
4790:function deriveSelectorGroup(hostname: string, fields: string): string {
4791:  const hash = createHash('sha256')
4792:    .update(fields.trim().toLowerCase())
4793:    .digest('hex')
4794:    .slice(0, 8);
4795:  return `${hostname}:${hash}`;
4796:}
4797:
4798:async function executeScrapeStructured(
4799:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
4800:  context: SkillExecutionContext
4801:): Promise<unknown> {
4802:  const url = String(input.url ?? '');
4803:  const fields = String(input.fields ?? '');
4804:  const remember = input.remember !== false; // default true
4805:  const selectorGroupInput = input.selector_group ? String(input.selector_group) : null;
4806:
4807:  if (!url) return { success: false, error: 'url is required' };
4808:  if (!fields) return { success: false, error: 'fields is required' };
4809:
4810:  let hostname: string;
4811:  try {
4812:    hostname = new URL(url).hostname;
4813:  } catch {
4814:    return { success: false, error: `Invalid URL: ${url}` };
4815:  }
4816:
4817:  const selectorGroup = selectorGroupInput ?? deriveSelectorGroup(hostname, fields);
4818:  const urlPattern = hostname; // Use hostname as URL pattern for Phase 2
4819:
4820:  // Canonicalize field names
4821:  const canonicalFields = fields
4822:    .split(',')
4823:    .map(f => canonicalizeFieldKey(f))
4824:    .filter(Boolean);
4825:
4826:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 1. Check for existing selectors ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
4827:  const storedSelectors = await loadSelectors({
4828:    orgId: context.organisationId,
4829:    subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4830:    urlPattern,
4831:    selectorGroup,
4832:  });
4833:
4834:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 2. Fetch the page (max Tier 2 ŌĆö need raw HTML for DOM extraction) ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
4835:  const scrapeResult = await scrapingEngine.scrape({
4836:    url,
4837:    outputFormat: 'text',
4838:    maxTier: 2,
4839:    orgId: context.organisationId,
4840:    subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? undefined,
4841:  });
4842:
4843:  if (!scrapeResult.success || !scrapeResult.rawHtml) {
4844:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to fetch page: ${url}` };
4845:  }
4846:
4847:  const contentHash = computeContentHash(scrapeResult.content);
4848:
4849:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 3a. Stored selectors exist ŌĆö DOM extraction path ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
4850:  if (storedSelectors.length > 0) {
4851:    try {
4852:      const { JSDOM } = await import('jsdom');
4853:      const { document } = new JSDOM(scrapeResult.rawHtml!).window;
4854:
4855:      const extracted: Record<string, string[]> = {};
4856:      let overallScore = 1.0;
4857:      let adaptiveMatchUsed = false;
4858:      let selectorUncertain = false;
4859:      const selectorUpdates: Array<{ id: string; newSelector: string; newFingerprint: import('./scrapingEngine/adaptiveSelector.js').ElementFingerprint }> = [];
4860:
4861:      for (const stored of storedSelectors) {
4862:        const fieldKey = stored.selectorName;
4863:        const resolution = resolveSelector(document, stored.cssSelector, stored.elementFingerprint);
4864:
4865:        if (!resolution.found) {
4866:          await incrementMiss(stored.id);
4867:          extracted[fieldKey] = [];
4868:          overallScore = Math.min(overallScore, 0);
4869:          continue;
4870:        }
4871:
4872:        if (resolution.adaptiveMatchUsed) {
4873:          adaptiveMatchUsed = true;
4874:          if (resolution.cssSelector && resolution.fingerprint) {
4875:            selectorUpdates.push({
4876:              id: stored.id,
4877:              newSelector: resolution.cssSelector,
4878:              newFingerprint: resolution.fingerprint,
4879:            });
4880:          }
4881:        }
4882:
4883:        overallScore = Math.min(overallScore, resolution.score);
4884:        if (resolution.uncertain) selectorUncertain = true;
4885:
4886:        // Extract all matching elements for this selector (per-field try/catch
4887:        // so a broken selector for one field doesn't discard the rest)
4888:        try {
4889:          const matchedEls = document.querySelectorAll(resolution.cssSelector!);
4890:          const values: string[] = [];
4891:          matchedEls.forEach((el: Element) => {
4892:            const text = (el.textContent ?? '').trim();
4893:            if (text) values.push(text);
4894:          });
4895:          extracted[fieldKey] = values;
4896:          await incrementHit(stored.id);
4897:        } catch {
4898:          await incrementMiss(stored.id);
4899:          extracted[fieldKey] = [];
4900:          overallScore = Math.min(overallScore, 0);
4901:        }
4902:      }
4903:
4904:      // Apply adaptive updates if any
4905:      for (const upd of selectorUpdates) {
4906:        await updateSelector(upd.id, upd.newSelector, upd.newFingerprint);
4907:      }
4908:
4909:      return {
4910:        success: true,
4911:        ...extracted,
4912:        selector_confidence: overallScore,
4913:        adaptive_match_used: adaptiveMatchUsed,
4914:        selector_uncertain: selectorUncertain,
4915:        content_hash: contentHash,
4916:        url,
4917:      };
4918:    } catch (err) {
4919:      // If DOM extraction fails, fall through to LLM path
4920:      const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
4921:      console.warn(`[scrape_structured] DOM extraction failed, falling back to LLM: ${errMsg}`);
4922:    }
4923:  }
4924:
4925:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 3b. No stored selectors ŌĆö LLM extraction path ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
4926:  // Build a focused DOM excerpt for the LLM
4927:  const htmlForLlm = (scrapeResult.rawHtml ?? '').slice(0, SCRAPE_STRUCTURED_MAX_HTML_CHARS);
4928:  const fieldList = canonicalFields.join(', ');
4929:
4930:  const extractionPrompt = `You are a data extraction assistant. Given the HTML below, extract structured data.
4931:
4932:Fields to extract: ${fieldList}
4933:
4934:Rules:
4935:- Return ONLY valid JSON with exactly these keys: ${fieldList}
4936:- Each key maps to an ARRAY of values (even if there is only one value)
4937:- For multiple records on the page (e.g. pricing tiers), each field array has one entry per record in the same order
4938:- Also return a "css_selectors" key mapping each field to the CSS selector that targets those elements
4939:- If a field cannot be found, use an empty array []
4940:
4941:Example response for fields "plan_name, price":
4942:{"plan_name":["Starter","Pro"],"price":["$9","$29"],"css_selectors":{"plan_name":"h3.plan-name","price":"span.price"}}
4943:
4944:HTML:
4945:${htmlForLlm}`;
4946:
4947:  const llmResponse = await routeCall({
4948:    messages: [{ role: 'user', content: extractionPrompt }],
4949:    maxTokens: 2000,
4950:    context: {
4951:      organisationId: context.organisationId,
4952:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? '',
4953:      runId: context.runId,
4954:      sourceType: 'system',
4955:      agentName: 'scrape_structured',
4956:      taskType: 'general',
4957:      routingMode: 'ceiling',
4958:    },
4959:  });
4960:
4961:  // Parse LLM response
4962:  let extracted: Record<string, unknown> = {};
4963:  let cssSelectorsFromLlm: Record<string, string> = {};
4964:
4965:  try {
4966:    const responseText = typeof llmResponse.content === 'string' ? llmResponse.content : '';
4967:    const jsonMatch = responseText.match(/\{[\s\S]*\}/);
4968:    if (jsonMatch) {
4969:      const parsed = JSON.parse(jsonMatch[0]) as Record<string, unknown>;
4970:      cssSelectorsFromLlm = (parsed.css_selectors as Record<string, string>) ?? {};
4971:      delete parsed.css_selectors;
4972:      extracted = parsed;
4973:    }
4974:  } catch {
4975:    return { success: false, error: 'LLM extraction failed to return valid JSON' };
4976:  }
4977:
4978:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 4. Learn selectors for next time ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
4979:  if (remember && Object.keys(cssSelectorsFromLlm).length > 0 && scrapeResult.rawHtml) {
4980:    try {
4981:      const { JSDOM } = await import('jsdom');
4982:      const { document: learnDoc } = new JSDOM(scrapeResult.rawHtml).window;
4983:
4984:      for (const [fieldName, selector] of Object.entries(cssSelectorsFromLlm)) {
4985:        if (!selector || typeof selector !== 'string') continue;
4986:        let el: Element | null = null;
4987:        try { el = learnDoc.querySelector(selector); } catch { continue; }
4988:        if (el === null) continue;
4989:
4990:        const fingerprint = buildFingerprint(el);
4991:
4992:        await saveSelector({
4993:          orgId: context.organisationId,
4994:          subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? null,
4995:          urlPattern,
4996:          selectorGroup,
4997:          selectorName: fieldName,
4998:          cssSelector: selector,
4999:          fingerprint,
5000:        }).catch(err => {
5001:          console.warn(`[scrape_structured] Failed to save selector for "${fieldName}": ${err}`);
5002:        });
5003:      }
5004:    } catch (err) {
5005:      // Selector learning is best-effort ŌĆö don't fail the extraction
5006:      console.warn(`[scrape_structured] Selector learning failed: ${err}`);
5007:    }
5008:  }
5009:
5010:  const dataWasTruncated = JSON.stringify(extracted).length > SCRAPE_STRUCTURED_RETURN_LIMIT;
5011:
5012:  return {
5013:    success: true,
5014:    ...extracted,
5015:    ...(dataWasTruncated ? { data_truncated: true } : {}),
5016:    selector_confidence: 0,        // 0 = LLM extraction (no stored selectors)
5017:    adaptive_match_used: false,
5018:    selector_uncertain: false,
5019:    content_hash: contentHash,
5020:    url,
5021:  };
5022:}

5024:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5025:// Monitor Webpage ŌĆö set up recurring monitoring with change detection
5026:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5027:
5028:const MONITOR_SCHEDULE_TIME_DEFAULT = '00:00';
5029:
5030:async function executeMonitorWebpage(
5031:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5032:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5033:): Promise<unknown> {
5034:  const url = String(input.url ?? '');
5035:  const watchFor = String(input.watch_for ?? '');
5036:  const frequency = String(input.frequency ?? '');
5037:  const fields = input.fields ? String(input.fields) : null;
5038:
5039:  if (!url) return { success: false, error: 'url is required' };
5040:  if (!watchFor) return { success: false, error: 'watch_for is required' };
5041:  if (!frequency) return { success: false, error: 'frequency is required' };
5042:
5043:  // requireSubaccountContext check ŌĆö monitor_webpage needs a subaccount to attach the scheduled task
5044:  if (!context.subaccountId) {
5045:    return { success: false, error: 'monitor_webpage requires a subaccount context' };
5046:  }
5047:
5048:  let hostname: string;
5049:  try {
5050:    hostname = new URL(url).hostname;
5051:  } catch {
5052:    return { success: false, error: `Invalid URL: ${url}` };
5053:  }
5054:
5055:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 0. Deduplication ŌĆö return existing task if one already monitors this URL ŌöĆŌöĆ
5056:  const existingTasks = await db
5057:    .select({ id: scheduledTasks.id, brief: scheduledTasks.brief })
5058:    .from(scheduledTasks)
5059:    .where(
5060:      and(
5061:        eq(scheduledTasks.organisationId, context.organisationId),
5062:        eq(scheduledTasks.subaccountId, context.subaccountId),
5063:        eq(scheduledTasks.assignedAgentId, context.agentId),
5064:        eq(scheduledTasks.isActive, true),
5065:      ),
5066:    );
5067:
5068:  const duplicate = existingTasks.find(t => {
5069:    try {
5070:      return parseMonitorBrief(t.brief ?? '').monitorUrl === url;
5071:    } catch {
5072:      return false;
5073:    }
5074:  });
5075:
5076:  if (duplicate) {
5077:    return {
5078:      success: true,
5079:      scheduled_task_id: duplicate.id,
5080:      already_existed: true,
5081:      message: `Monitor for ${url} already exists (task ${duplicate.id})`,
5082:    };
5083:  }
5084:
5085:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 1. Parse frequency to rrule ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
5086:  let rrule: string;
5087:  try {
