5089:  } catch (err) {
5090:    const msg = (err as { message?: string })?.message ?? `Unsupported frequency: "${frequency}"`;
5091:    return { success: false, error: msg };
5092:  }
5093:
5094:  // Derive scheduleTime from rrule (default 00:00 for simple frequencies)
5095:  const scheduleTime = MONITOR_SCHEDULE_TIME_DEFAULT;
5096:
5097:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 2. Derive selectorGroup ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
5098:  let selectorGroup: string | null = null;
5099:  if (fields) {
5100:    selectorGroup = deriveSelectorGroup(hostname, fields);
5101:  }
5102:
5103:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 3. Establish initial baseline ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
5104:  let baselineContentHash: string;
5105:  let baselineExtractedData: Record<string, unknown> | null = null;
5106:
5107:  if (fields) {
5108:    // Structured monitoring ŌĆö use LLM extraction for first run
5109:    const structuredResult = await executeScrapeStructured(
5110:      { url, fields, remember: true, selector_group: selectorGroup },
5111:      context
5112:    ) as Record<string, unknown>;
5113:
5114:    if (structuredResult.success === false) {
5115:      return {
5116:        success: false,
5117:        error: `Failed to establish structured baseline: ${structuredResult.error}`,
5118:      };
5119:    }
5120:
5121:    baselineContentHash = String(structuredResult.content_hash ?? '');
5122:    const {
5123:      success: _s,
5124:      content_hash: _ch,
5125:      url: _u,
5126:      selector_confidence: _sc,
5127:      adaptive_match_used: _am,
5128:      selector_uncertain: _su,
5129:      data_truncated: _dt,
5130:      ...dataFields
5131:    } = structuredResult;
5132:    baselineExtractedData = dataFields as Record<string, unknown>;
5133:  } else {
5134:    // Hash-based monitoring
5135:    const scrapeResult = await scrapingEngine.scrape({
5136:      url,
5137:      outputFormat: 'markdown',
5138:      orgId: context.organisationId,
5139:      subaccountId: context.subaccountId ?? undefined,
5140:    });
5141:
5142:    if (!scrapeResult.success) {
5143:      return { success: false, error: `Failed to establish baseline ŌĆö page could not be fetched: ${url}` };
5144:    }
5145:
5146:    baselineContentHash = scrapeResult.contentHash;
5147:  }
5148:
5149:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 4. Create scheduled task ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
5150:  // The brief carries all config needed by subsequent runs.
5151:  // A temporary ID placeholder ŌĆö replaced after insert with actual ID.
5152:  const briefPlaceholder = serializeMonitorBrief({
5153:    type: 'monitor_webpage_run',
5154:    monitorUrl: url,
5155:    watchFor,
5156:    fields,
5157:    selectorGroup,
5158:    scheduledTaskId: '__PLACEHOLDER__',
5159:  });
5160:
5161:  const title = `Monitor: ${hostname} ŌĆö ${watchFor.slice(0, 50)}`;
5162:
5163:  const scheduledTask = await scheduledTaskService.create(
5164:    context.organisationId,
5165:    context.subaccountId,
5166:    {
5167:      title,
5168:      brief: briefPlaceholder, // updated below
5169:      assignedAgentId: context.agentId, // Strategic Intelligence Agent
5170:      rrule,
5171:      timezone: 'UTC',
5172:      scheduleTime,
5173:    },
5174:  );
5175:
5176:  // ŌöĆŌöĆ 5. Update brief with actual scheduledTaskId ŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆŌöĆ
5177:  const finalBrief = serializeMonitorBrief({
5178:    type: 'monitor_webpage_run',
5179:    monitorUrl: url,
5180:    watchFor,
5181:    fields,
5182:    selectorGroup,
5183:    scheduledTaskId: scheduledTask.id,
5184:    baseline: {
5185:      contentHash: baselineContentHash,
5186:      extractedData: baselineExtractedData,
5187:    },
5188:  });
5189:
5190:  await scheduledTaskService.update(scheduledTask.id, context.organisationId, { brief: finalBrief });
5191:
5192:  return {
5193:    success: true,
5194:    scheduled_task_id: scheduledTask.id,
5195:    title,
5196:    rrule,
5197:    frequency,
5198:    url,
5199:    watch_for: watchFor,
5200:    fields: fields ?? null,
5201:    baseline_content_hash: baselineContentHash,
5202:    message: `Monitoring scheduled. The "${title}" task will run ${frequency} and alert you when ${watchFor} changes.`,
5203:  };
5204:}

5206:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5207:// proposeDevopsAction ŌĆö safeMode-checked proposal for write_patch / run_command / create_pr
5208:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5209:
5210:async function proposeDevopsAction(
5211:  actionType: 'write_patch' | 'run_command' | 'create_pr',
5212:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5213:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5214:): Promise<unknown> {
5215:  let devCtxResult;
5216:  try {
5217:    devCtxResult = await devContextService.getContext(context.subaccountId!);
5218:  } catch (err) {
5219:    const msg = (err as { message?: string }).message ?? String(err);
5220:    return { success: false, error: `Cannot load dev execution context: ${msg}` };
5221:  }
5222:
5223:  const { context: devCtx } = devCtxResult;
5224:
5225:  // safeMode blocks all code-modification actions
5226:  if (devCtx.safeMode) {
5227:    return {
5228:      success: false,
5229:      error: `safeMode is enabled for this subaccount. ${actionType} is not allowed. Disable safeMode in devContext settings to permit code changes.`,
5230:      errorCode: 'permission_failure',
5231:    };
5232:  }
5233:
5234:  // write_patch: validate patchLimits + maxPatchAttemptsPerTask before proposing
5235:  if (actionType === 'write_patch') {
5236:    const diff = String(input.diff ?? '');
5237:    const lineCount = diff.split('\n').length;
5238:    if (lineCount > devCtx.patchLimits.maxLinesChanged) {
5239:      return {
5240:        success: false,
5241:        error: `Patch exceeds maxLinesChanged limit (${lineCount} lines > ${devCtx.patchLimits.maxLinesChanged}). Split the change into smaller patches.`,
5242:        errorCode: 'patch_size_exceeded',
5243:      };
5244:    }
5245:
5246:    // Enforce maxPatchAttemptsPerTask across all runs for this task
5247:    if (context.taskId) {
5248:      const taskRunRows = await db
5249:        .select({ id: agentRuns.id })
5250:        .from(agentRuns)
5251:        .where(eq(agentRuns.taskId, context.taskId));
5252:      const taskRunIds = taskRunRows.map(r => r.id);
5253:      const patchCount = taskRunIds.length
5254:        ? await db
5255:            .select({ total: count() })
5256:            .from(actions)
5257:            .where(and(inArray(actions.agentRunId, taskRunIds), eq(actions.actionType, 'write_patch')))
5258:            .then(rows => Number(rows[0]?.total ?? 0))
5259:        : 0;
5260:      if (patchCount >= devCtx.costLimits.maxPatchAttemptsPerTask) {
5261:        return {
5262:          success: false,
5263:          error: `Patch attempt limit reached (${patchCount}/${devCtx.costLimits.maxPatchAttemptsPerTask} per task). Cannot propose more patches for this task without human review.`,
5264:          errorCode: 'permission_failure',
5265:        };
5266:      }
5267:    }
5268:
5269:    // Auto-inject task_id so devopsAdapter can manage the correct branch
5270:    if (context.taskId) {
5271:      input = { ...input, task_id: context.taskId };
5272:    }
5273:  }
5274:
5275:  // run_command: enforce maxCommandsPerRun cost limit
5276:  if (actionType === 'run_command') {
5277:    const [countRow] = await db
5278:      .select({ total: count() })
5279:      .from(actions)
5280:      .where(
5281:        and(
5282:          eq(actions.agentRunId, context.runId),
5283:          eq(actions.actionType, 'run_command')
5284:        )
5285:      );
5286:    const commandCount = Number(countRow?.total ?? 0);
5287:    if (commandCount >= devCtx.costLimits.maxCommandsPerRun) {
5288:      return {
5289:        success: false,
5290:        error: `Command limit reached (${commandCount}/${devCtx.costLimits.maxCommandsPerRun} per run). Cannot run more commands in this agent run.`,
5291:        errorCode: 'permission_failure',
5292:      };
5293:    }
5294:  }
5295:
5296:  return proposeReviewGatedAction(actionType, input, context);
5297:}

5299:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5300:// Read Codebase ŌĆö read a file from DEC projectRoot with path validation
5301:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5302:
5303:const READ_CODEBASE_MAX_BYTES = 50 * 1024; // 50 KB
5304:
5305:async function executeReadCodebase(
5306:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5307:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5308:): Promise<unknown> {
5309:  const filePath = String(input.file_path ?? '');
5310:  if (!filePath) return { success: false, error: 'file_path is required' };
5311:
5312:  try {
5313:    const { context: devCtx } = await devContextService.getContext(context.subaccountId!);
5314:    const absolutePath = resolve(devCtx.projectRoot, filePath);
5315:
5316:    assertPathInRoot(absolutePath, devCtx.projectRoot);
5317:
5318:    const raw = await readFile(absolutePath, 'utf8');
5319:    const rawBytes = Buffer.byteLength(raw, 'utf8');
5320:    const truncated = rawBytes > READ_CODEBASE_MAX_BYTES;
5321:    const content = truncated
5322:      ? Buffer.from(raw, 'utf8').slice(0, READ_CODEBASE_MAX_BYTES).toString('utf8')
5323:      : raw;
5324:
5325:    return {
5326:      success: true,
5327:      file_path: filePath,
5328:      content,
5329:      truncated,
5330:      size_bytes: rawBytes,
5331:    };
5332:  } catch (err) {
5333:    const e = err as { message?: string; code?: string; statusCode?: number };
5334:    if (e.statusCode === 403) return { success: false, error: e.message ?? 'Access denied' };
5335:    if (e.code === 'ENOENT') return { success: false, error: `File not found: ${filePath}` };
5336:    return { success: false, error: e.message ?? String(err) };
5337:  }
5338:}
5339:
5340:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5341:// Search Codebase ŌĆö grep content or glob filenames, scoped to projectRoot
5342:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5343:
5344:async function executeSearchCodebase(
5345:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5346:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5347:): Promise<unknown> {
5348:  const query = String(input.query ?? '');
5349:  const searchType = String(input.search_type ?? 'content'); // 'content' | 'filename'
5350:  const filePattern = input.file_pattern ? String(input.file_pattern) : undefined;
5351:  const maxResults = Math.min(Number(input.max_results ?? 20), 50);
5352:
5353:  if (!query) return { success: false, error: 'query is required' };
5354:
5355:  try {
5356:    const { context: devCtx } = await devContextService.getContext(context.subaccountId!);
5357:    const root = devCtx.projectRoot;
5358:
5359:    if (searchType === 'filename') {
5360:      const pattern = filePattern ?? `**/*${query}*`;
5361:      const matches: string[] = [];
5362:      for (const file of await glob(pattern, { cwd: root })) {
5363:        const strFile = String(file);
5364:        matches.push(strFile);
5365:        if (matches.length >= maxResults) break;
5366:      }
5367:      return {
5368:        success: true,
5369:        search_type: 'filename',
5370:        query,
5371:        results: matches.map(f => ({ file: f })),
5372:        total: matches.length,
5373:      };
5374:    }
5375:
5376:    // Content search using grep
5377:    const includeArg = filePattern ? `--include=${filePattern}` : '--include=*';
5378:    const grepArgs = ['-r', '-n', '--max-count=5', includeArg, query, root];
5379:
5380:    const { stdout } = await execFileAsync('grep', grepArgs, {
5381:      cwd: root,
5382:      timeout: 30000,
5383:      maxBuffer: 1024 * 1024,
5384:    }).catch((err: { stdout?: string; code?: number }) => {
5385:      // grep exits 1 when no matches ŌĆö not a real failure
5386:      if (err.code === 1) return { stdout: '' };
5387:      throw err;
5388:    });
5389:
5390:    const lines = stdout.trim().split('\n').filter(Boolean);
5391:    const results = lines.slice(0, maxResults).map(line => {
5392:      const colonIdx = line.indexOf(':');
5393:      const secondColon = line.indexOf(':', colonIdx + 1);
5394:      const file = line.slice(root.length + 1, colonIdx);
5395:      const lineNum = secondColon !== -1 ? line.slice(colonIdx + 1, secondColon) : '';
5396:      const content = secondColon !== -1 ? line.slice(secondColon + 1) : line.slice(colonIdx + 1);
5397:      return { file, line: lineNum ? Number(lineNum) : undefined, content: content.trim() };
5398:    });
5399:
5400:    return {
5401:      success: true,
5402:      search_type: 'content',
5403:      query,
5404:      results,
5405:      total: results.length,
5406:      truncated: lines.length > maxResults,
5407:    };
5408:  } catch (err) {
5409:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
5410:    return { success: false, error: `Search failed: ${errMsg}` };
5411:  }
5412:}
5413:
5414:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5415:// Run Tests ŌĆö execute DEC testCommand, enforce maxTestRunsPerTask limit
5416:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5417:
5418:async function executeRunTests(
5419:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5420:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5421:): Promise<unknown> {
5422:  let devCtxResult;
5423:  try {
5424:    devCtxResult = await devContextService.getContext(context.subaccountId!);
5425:  } catch (err) {
5426:    const msg = (err as { message?: string }).message ?? String(err);
5427:    return { success: false, error: `Cannot load dev execution context: ${msg}` };
5428:  }
5429:
5430:  const { context: devCtx } = devCtxResult;
5431:
5432:  // Enforce maxTestRunsPerTask cost limit
5433:  // actions table has no taskId column; count via agentRuns.taskId ŌåÆ actions.agentRunId
5434:  if (context.taskId) {
5435:    const taskRunRows = await db
5436:      .select({ id: agentRuns.id })
5437:      .from(agentRuns)
5438:      .where(eq(agentRuns.taskId, context.taskId));
5439:    const taskRunIds = taskRunRows.map(r => r.id);
5440:    const runCount = taskRunIds.length
5441:      ? await db
5442:          .select({ total: count() })
5443:          .from(actions)
5444:          .where(and(inArray(actions.agentRunId, taskRunIds), eq(actions.actionType, 'run_tests')))
5445:          .then(rows => Number(rows[0]?.total ?? 0))
5446:      : 0;
5447:    if (runCount >= devCtx.costLimits.maxTestRunsPerTask) {
5448:      return {
5449:        success: false,
5450:        error: `Test run limit reached (${runCount}/${devCtx.costLimits.maxTestRunsPerTask} per task). Cannot run more tests for this task.`,
5451:        errorCode: 'permission_failure',
5452:      };
5453:    }
5454:  }
5455:
5456:  const testFilter = input.test_filter ? String(input.test_filter) : undefined;
5457:  const baseCommand = devCtx.testCommand;
5458:  const command = testFilter ? `${baseCommand} ${testFilter}` : baseCommand;
5459:
5460:  const [cmd, ...args] = command.split(' ');
5461:  const start = Date.now();
5462:
5463:  try {
5464:    const { stdout, stderr } = await execFileAsync(cmd, args, {
5465:      cwd: devCtx.projectRoot,
5466:      timeout: devCtx.resourceLimits.commandTimeoutMs,
5467:      maxBuffer: devCtx.resourceLimits.maxOutputBytes,
5468:      env: { ...process.env, ...devCtx.env },
5469:    }).catch((err: { stdout?: string; stderr?: string; code?: number }) => {
5470:      // Non-zero exit = test failures; still capture output
5471:      return { stdout: err.stdout ?? '', stderr: err.stderr ?? '' };
5472:    });
5473:
5474:    const durationMs = Date.now() - start;
5475:    const output = (stdout + (stderr ? `\nSTDERR:\n${stderr}` : '')).slice(
5476:      0,
5477:      devCtx.resourceLimits.maxOutputBytes
5478:    );
5479:    const truncated = (stdout + stderr).length > devCtx.resourceLimits.maxOutputBytes;
5480:
5481:    // Basic pass/fail detection from output
5482:    const passed = /\d+ passed/.exec(output)?.[0] ?? null;
5483:    const failed = /\d+ failed/.exec(output)?.[0] ?? null;
5484:
5485:    return {
5486:      success: true,
5487:      command,
5488:      output,
5489:      truncated,
5490:      duration_ms: durationMs,
5491:      passed,
5492:      failed,
5493:    };
5494:  } catch (err) {
5495:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
5496:    return { success: false, error: `Test execution failed: ${errMsg}` };
5497:  }
5498:}
5499:
5500:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5501:// Analyze Endpoint ŌĆö HTTP request with timing and expected-status validation
5502:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5503:
5504:async function executeAnalyzeEndpoint(
5505:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5506:  _context: SkillExecutionContext
5507:): Promise<unknown> {
5508:  const url = String(input.url ?? '');
5509:  if (!url) return { success: false, error: 'url is required' };
5510:
5511:  const method = String(input.method ?? 'GET').toUpperCase();
5512:  const expectedStatus = input.expected_status ? Number(input.expected_status) : undefined;
5513:  const headers: Record<string, string> = {};
5514:  if (input.headers && typeof input.headers === 'object') {
5515:    for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(input.headers as Record<string, unknown>)) {
5516:      headers[k] = String(v);
5517:    }
5518:  }
5519:
5520:  const start = Date.now();
5521:
5522:  try {
5523:    const fetchOptions: RequestInit = {
5524:      method,
5525:      headers,
5526:      signal: AbortSignal.timeout(30_000),
5527:    };
5528:
5529:    if ((method === 'POST' || method === 'PUT' || method === 'PATCH') && input.body) {
5530:      fetchOptions.body = String(input.body);
5531:      if (!headers['Content-Type'] && !headers['content-type']) {
5532:        headers['Content-Type'] = 'application/json';
5533:      }
5534:    }
5535:
5536:    const response = await fetch(url, fetchOptions);
5537:    const durationMs = Date.now() - start;
5538:    const bodyText = await response.text();
5539:    const truncated = bodyText.length > 10000;
5540:    const content = truncated ? bodyText.slice(0, 10000) : bodyText;
5541:
5542:    const statusOk = expectedStatus !== undefined
5543:      ? response.status === expectedStatus
5544:      : response.ok;
5545:
5546:    return {
5547:      success: true,
5548:      url,
5549:      method,
5550:      status_code: response.status,
5551:      status_ok: statusOk,
5552:      expected_status: expectedStatus,
5553:      content,
5554:      truncated,
5555:      content_type: response.headers.get('content-type') ?? undefined,
5556:      duration_ms: durationMs,
5557:      headers: Object.fromEntries(response.headers.entries()),
5558:    };
5559:  } catch (err) {
5560:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
5561:    return { success: false, error: `Endpoint analysis failed: ${errMsg}`, duration_ms: Date.now() - start };
5562:  }
5563:}

5565:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5566:// Report Bug ŌĆö create a structured board task with severity/confidence metadata
5567:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5568:
5569:async function executeReportBug(
5570:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5571:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5572:): Promise<unknown> {
5573:  const title = String(input.title ?? '').slice(0, MAX_TASK_TITLE_LENGTH);
5574:  if (!title) return { success: false, error: 'title is required' };
5575:
5576:  const description = input.description ? String(input.description).slice(0, MAX_TASK_DESCRIPTION_LENGTH) : undefined;
5577:  const severity = String(input.severity ?? 'medium'); // low | medium | high | critical
5578:  const confidence = Number(input.confidence ?? 0.8);
5579:  const stepsToReproduce = input.steps_to_reproduce ? String(input.steps_to_reproduce) : undefined;
5580:  const expectedBehavior = input.expected_behavior ? String(input.expected_behavior) : undefined;
5581:  const actualBehavior = input.actual_behavior ? String(input.actual_behavior) : undefined;
5582:
5583:  const brief = [
5584:    description,
5585:    stepsToReproduce ? `**Steps to reproduce:**\n${stepsToReproduce}` : null,
5586:    expectedBehavior ? `**Expected:** ${expectedBehavior}` : null,
5587:    actualBehavior ? `**Actual:** ${actualBehavior}` : null,
5588:    `**Severity:** ${severity}`,
5589:    `**Confidence:** ${(confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}%`,
5590:  ]
5591:    .filter(Boolean)
5592:    .join('\n\n')
5593:    .slice(0, MAX_TASK_DESCRIPTION_LENGTH);
5594:
5595:  // Map severity to task priority
5596:  const priorityMap: Record<string, string> = {
5597:    critical: 'urgent',
5598:    high: 'high',
5599:    medium: 'normal',
5600:    low: 'low',
5601:  };
5602:  const priority = (priorityMap[severity] ?? 'normal') as 'urgent' | 'high' | 'normal' | 'low';
5603:
5604:  try {
5605:    const tx = getOrgScopedDb('service:skillExecutor.executeReportBug');
5606:    const task = await taskService.createTask(
5607:      {
5608:        organisationId: context.organisationId,
5609:        subaccountId: context.subaccountId!,
5610:        data: {
5611:          title: `[BUG] ${title}`,
5612:          description,
5613:          brief,
5614:          status: 'inbox',
5615:          priority,
5616:          createdByAgentId: context.agentId,
5617:        },
5618:      },
5619:      tx,
5620:    );
5621:
5622:    await taskService.addActivity(task.id, context.organisationId, {
5623:      activityType: 'note',
5624:      message: `Bug reported by QA agent ŌĆö severity: ${severity}, confidence: ${(confidence * 100).toFixed(0)}%`,
5625:      agentId: context.agentId,
5626:    });
5627:
5628:    return {
5629:      success: true,
5630:      task_id: task.id,
5631:      title: task.title,
5632:      severity,
5633:      confidence,
5634:      _created_task: true,
5635:    };
5636:  } catch (err) {
5637:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
5638:    return { success: false, error: `Failed to report bug: ${errMsg}` };
5639:  }
5640:}
5641:
5642:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5643:// Capture Screenshot ŌĆö launch headless browser, navigate, capture
5644:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5645:
5646:async function executeCaptureScreenshot(
5647:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5648:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5649:): Promise<unknown> {
5650:  let devCtxResult;
5651:  try {
5652:    devCtxResult = await devContextService.getContext(context.subaccountId!);
5653:  } catch (err) {
5654:    const msg = (err as { message?: string }).message ?? String(err);
5655:    return { success: false, error: `Cannot load dev execution context: ${msg}` };
5656:  }
5657:
5658:  const { context: devCtx } = devCtxResult;
5659:
5660:  if (!devCtx.playwright) {
5661:    return {
5662:      success: false,
5663:      error: 'Playwright is not configured for this subaccount. Add a "playwright" section to devContext settings with at minimum a baseUrl.',
5664:    };
5665:  }
5666:
5667:  const url = String(input.url ?? '');
5668:  if (!url) return { success: false, error: 'url is required' };
5669:
5670:  const reasoning = String(input.reasoning ?? '');
5671:  if (!reasoning) return { success: false, error: 'reasoning is required' };
5672:
5673:  const selector = input.selector ? String(input.selector) : null;
5674:  const viewport = input.viewport as { width?: number; height?: number } | undefined;
5675:
5676:  // Resolve screenshot output directory (must be inside projectRoot)
5677:  const screenshotDirRelative = devCtx.playwright.screenshotDir;
5678:  const screenshotDir = resolve(devCtx.projectRoot, screenshotDirRelative);
5679:  assertPathInRoot(screenshotDir, devCtx.projectRoot);
5680:
5681:  const timestamp = Date.now();
5682:  const filename = `screenshot_${timestamp}.png`;
5683:  const screenshotPath = join(screenshotDir, filename);
5684:
5685:  try {
5686:    const { mkdir } = await import('fs/promises');
5687:    await mkdir(screenshotDir, { recursive: true });
5688:
5689:    const playwright = await import('playwright');
5690:    const browserType = playwright[devCtx.playwright.browser] ?? playwright.chromium;
5691:
5692:    const browser = await browserType.launch({ headless: true });
5693:    try {
5694:      const page = await browser.newPage({
5695:        viewport: {
5696:          width: viewport?.width ?? 1280,
5697:          height: viewport?.height ?? 720,
5698:        },
5699:      });
5700:
5701:      page.setDefaultTimeout(devCtx.playwright.timeoutMs);
5702:
5703:      await page.goto(url, { waitUntil: 'networkidle', timeout: devCtx.playwright.timeoutMs });
5704:
5705:      let screenshotOptions: { path: string; fullPage?: boolean } = { path: screenshotPath };
5706:
5707:      if (selector) {
5708:        const element = await page.locator(selector).first();
5709:        const box = await element.boundingBox();
5710:        if (!box) return { success: false, error: `Selector "${selector}" found no visible element` };
5711:        await element.screenshot({ path: screenshotPath });
5712:      } else {
5713:        screenshotOptions = { path: screenshotPath, fullPage: !viewport };
5714:        await page.screenshot(screenshotOptions);
5715:      }
5716:
5717:      // Read back as base64 for inline delivery
5718:      const { readFile } = await import('fs/promises');
5719:      const imageBuffer = await readFile(screenshotPath);
5720:      const base64 = imageBuffer.toString('base64');
5721:
5722:      return {
5723:        success: true,
5724:        url,
5725:        selector: selector ?? null,
5726:        screenshot_path: screenshotPath.replace(devCtx.projectRoot, '').replace(/\\/g, '/'),
5727:        screenshot_base64: `data:image/png;base64,${base64}`,
5728:        size_bytes: imageBuffer.length,
5729:        reasoning,
5730:      };
5731:    } finally {
5732:      await browser.close();
5733:    }
5734:  } catch (err) {
5735:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
5736:    // Diagnose common failure: browsers not installed
5737:    if (errMsg.includes('Executable doesn\'t exist') || errMsg.includes('browserType.launch')) {
5738:      return {
5739:        success: false,
5740:        error: `Playwright browser binaries not installed. Run: npx playwright install ${devCtx.playwright.browser}. Original error: ${errMsg}`,
5741:      };
5742:    }
5743:    return { success: false, error: `Screenshot failed: ${errMsg}` };
5744:  }
5745:}

5747:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5748:// Run Playwright Test ŌĆö execute a specific Playwright test file via CLI
5749:// ---------------------------------------------------------------------------
5750:
5751:async function executeRunPlaywrightTest(
5752:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
5753:  context: SkillExecutionContext
5754:): Promise<unknown> {
5755:  let devCtxResult;
5756:  try {
5757:    devCtxResult = await devContextService.getContext(context.subaccountId!);
5758:  } catch (err) {
5759:    const msg = (err as { message?: string }).message ?? String(err);
5760:    return { success: false, error: `Cannot load dev execution context: ${msg}` };
5761:  }
5762:
5763:  const { context: devCtx } = devCtxResult;
5764:
5765:  if (!devCtx.playwright) {
5766:    return {
5767:      success: false,
5768:      error: 'Playwright is not configured for this subaccount. Add a "playwright" section to devContext settings with at minimum a baseUrl.',
5769:    };
5770:  }
5771:
5772:  // Enforce the same maxTestRunsPerTask limit as run_tests
5773:  if (context.taskId) {
5774:    const taskRunRows = await db
5775:      .select({ id: agentRuns.id })
5776:      .from(agentRuns)
5777:      .where(eq(agentRuns.taskId, context.taskId));
5778:    const taskRunIds = taskRunRows.map(r => r.id);
5779:    const runCount = taskRunIds.length
5780:      ? await db
5781:          .select({ total: count() })
5782:          .from(actions)
5783:          .where(and(inArray(actions.agentRunId, taskRunIds), eq(actions.actionType, 'run_playwright_test')))
5784:          .then(rows => Number(rows[0]?.total ?? 0))
5785:      : 0;
5786:    if (runCount >= devCtx.costLimits.maxTestRunsPerTask) {
5787:      return {
5788:        success: false,
5789:        error: `Playwright test run limit reached (${runCount}/${devCtx.costLimits.maxTestRunsPerTask} per task).`,
5790:        errorCode: 'permission_failure',
5791:      };
5792:    }
5793:  }
5794:
5795:  const testFile = String(input.test_file ?? '');
5796:  if (!testFile) return { success: false, error: 'test_file is required' };
5797:
5798:  const baseUrl = String(input.base_url ?? devCtx.playwright.baseUrl);
5799:  const testName = input.test_name ? String(input.test_name) : null;
5800:
5801:  // Validate test file is inside projectRoot
5802:  const absoluteTestPath = resolve(devCtx.projectRoot, testFile);
5803:  assertPathInRoot(absoluteTestPath, devCtx.projectRoot);
5804:
5805:  // Build the Playwright CLI command
5806:  const args = ['playwright', 'test', testFile, '--reporter=line'];
5807:  if (testName) args.push('--grep', testName);
5808:  // Pass baseUrl via env so playwright.config.ts can pick it up
5809:  const env = { ...process.env, ...devCtx.env, PLAYWRIGHT_BASE_URL: baseUrl, BASE_URL: baseUrl };
5810:
5811:  const start = Date.now();
5812:
5813:  try {
5814:    const { stdout, stderr } = await execFileAsync('npx', args, {
5815:      cwd: devCtx.projectRoot,
5816:      timeout: devCtx.playwright.timeoutMs * 3, // E2E tests take longer
5817:      maxBuffer: devCtx.resourceLimits.maxOutputBytes,
5818:      env,
5819:    }).catch((err: { stdout?: string; stderr?: string; code?: number }) => {
5820:      return { stdout: err.stdout ?? '', stderr: err.stderr ?? '' };
5821:    });
5822:
5823:    const durationMs = Date.now() - start;
5824:    const output = (stdout + (stderr ? `\nSTDERR:\n${stderr}` : '')).slice(0, devCtx.resourceLimits.maxOutputBytes);
5825:    const truncated = (stdout + stderr).length > devCtx.resourceLimits.maxOutputBytes;
5826:
5827:    const passed = /(\d+) passed/.exec(output)?.[1] ?? null;
5828:    const failed = /(\d+) failed/.exec(output)?.[1] ?? null;
5829:    const skipped = /(\d+) skipped/.exec(output)?.[1] ?? null;
5830:
5831:    return {
5832:      success: true,
5833:      test_file: testFile,
5834:      test_name: testName,
5835:      base_url: baseUrl,
5836:      output,
5837:      truncated,
5838:      duration_ms: durationMs,
5839:      passed: passed ? Number(passed) : null,
5840:      failed: failed ? Number(failed) : null,
5841:      skipped: skipped ? Number(skipped) : null,
5842:      all_passed: failed === null && passed !== null,
5843:    };
5844:  } catch (err) {
5845:    const errMsg = err instanceof Error ? err.message : String(err);
5846:    if (errMsg.includes('Executable doesn\'t exist') || errMsg.includes('browserType.launch')) {
5847:      return {
5848:        success: false,
5849:        error: `Playwright browser binaries not installed. Run: npx playwright install ${devCtx.playwright.browser}. Original error: ${errMsg}`,
5850:      };
5851:    }
5852:    return { success: false, error: `Playwright test execution failed: ${errMsg}` };
5853:  }
5854:}

6009:async function executeWorkflowProposeSave(
6010:  input: Record<string, unknown>,
6011:  context: SkillExecutionContext
6012:): Promise<unknown> {
6013:  // Definition-only API. The agent supplies the validated definition
6014:  // object (NOT raw file contents) and the server renders the
6015:  // .Workflow.ts file deterministically. There is no input the agent
6016:  // can use to inject arbitrary file content ŌĆö that's the whole point
6017:  // of spec invariant 14 in the post-round-3 design.
6018:  const sessionId = String(input.sessionId ?? '');
6019:  const definition = input.definition;
6020:  if (!sessionId) {
6021:    return { success: false, error: 'sessionId is required' };
6022:  }
6023:  if (!definition || typeof definition !== 'object') {
6024:    return {
6025:      success: false,
6026:      error:
6027:        'definition object is required. propose_save no longer accepts fileContents ŌĆö the server renders the Workflow file deterministically from the validated definition.',
6028:    };
6029:  }
6030:  // Feature 3 ┬¦5.6 ŌĆö high-severity gate for n8n imports.
6031:  // If the caller passes unresolved_high_severity_count > 0, the import
6032:  // session still has unacknowledged high-severity mapping items (disconnected
6033:  // nodes, unconvertible code/function nodes). Block until the admin resolves
6034:  // or explicitly dismisses each item.
6035:  if (
6036:    typeof input.unresolved_high_severity_count === 'number' &&
6037:    input.unresolved_high_severity_count > 0
6038:  ) {
6039:    return {
6040:      success: false,
6041:      error: `Cannot save: ${input.unresolved_high_severity_count} high-severity item(s) from the n8n import are unresolved. 6042:    };
6043:  }
6044:  // Strict user-scope enforcement (review finding #3 from the previous
6045:  // round). The agent run's initiating principal MUST be present on the
6046:  // SkillExecutionContext; if it's missing (e.g. a scheduled / system
6047:  // run that has no user identity), we refuse to write to user-owned
6048:  // session rows.
6049:  if (!context.userId) {
6050:    return {
6051:      success: false,
6052:      error:
6053:        'workflow_propose_save requires a user-scoped agent run. The current run has no userId on its SkillExecutionContext (likely a scheduled or system run). Studio sessions can only be modified by their owners.',
6054:    };
6055:  }
6056:  const { WorkflowStudioService: workflowStudioService } = await import('./workflowStudioService.js');
6057:  // Validate + render in one call. This re-uses the exact same code
6058:  // path the /render endpoint uses, so the server's view of the
6059:  // canonical file body is consistent everywhere.
6060:  const rendered = workflowStudioService.validateAndRender(definition);
6061:  if (!rendered.ok) {
6062:    return {
6063:      success: false,
6064:      error: 'Definition failed validation',
6065:      validationErrors: rendered.errors,
6066:    };
6067:  }
6068:  // Persist the rendered file as the session's candidate, scoped by
6069:  // (sessionId, userId). Returns false when the session doesn't exist
6070:  // OR isn't owned by the calling user.
6071:  const updated = await workflowStudioService.updateCandidate(
6072:    sessionId,
6073:    context.userId,
6074:    rendered.fileContents,
6075:    'valid'
6076:  );
6077:  if (!updated) {
6078:    return {
6079:      success: false,
6080:      error:
6081:        'Session not found or not owned by the calling user. The agent can only update its own session.',
6082:    };
6083:  }
6084:  return {
6085:    success: true,
6086:    message:
6087:      'Candidate rendered and recorded. The human admin must click Save & Open PR in the Studio UI to commit this file via their GitHub identity.',
6088:    sessionId,
6089:    definitionHash: rendered.definitionHash,
6090:  };
6091:}
